-- Fonction sÃ©curisÃ©e pour copier dans le presse-papiers
local function copyToClipboard(str)
    if setclipboard then
        setclipboard(str)
        return true
    elseif toclipboard then
        toclipboard(str)
        return true
    end
    return false
end

local function SendNotification(text, duration)
    task.spawn(function()
        local NotifGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
        NotifGui.Name = "CyberpunksNotification"
        pcall(function() NotifGui.Parent = CoreGui end)
        if not NotifGui.Parent then NotifGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui") end
        
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 260, 0, 40)
        Frame.Position = UDim2.new(1, 270, 1, -60)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 10, 12)
        Frame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.25
        Frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Frame.Parent = NotifGui
        
        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner") Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) Corner.Parent = Frame
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) Stroke.Thickness = 1 Stroke.Transparency = 0.8 Stroke.Parent = Frame
        
        local Accent = Instance.new("Frame")
        Accent.Size = UDim2.new(0, 2, 0.6, 0)
        Accent.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0.2, 0)
        Accent.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        Accent.BorderSizePixel = 0
        Accent.Parent = Frame
        local ACorner = Instance.new("UICorner") ACorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0) ACorner.Parent = Accent
        
        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, -25, 1, 0)
        Label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 18, 0, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.Text = text
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(240, 240, 240)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextSize = 10
        Label.TextWrapped = true
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        TweenService:Create(Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Position = UDim2.new(1, -280, 1, -60)}):Play()
        task.wait(duration)
        local tween = TweenService:Create(Frame, TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Position = UDim2.new(1, 270, 1, -60)})
        tween:Play()
        tween.Completed:Wait()
        NotifGui:Destroy()
    end)
end

local PartViewerEnabled = false

local function StartPartViewer()
    PartViewerEnabled = true
    SendNotification("Part Viewer started! Check F9 console for object names", 5)
    
    task.spawn(function()
        while PartViewerEnabled do
            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("Tool") then
                    print("[PART VIEWER] Tool: " .. v.Name .. " | Parent: " .. v.Parent.Name .. " | ToolTip: " .. (v.ToolTip or "None"))
                elseif v:IsA("Model") and v:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
                    print("[PART VIEWER] Model with Handle: " .. v.Name .. " | Parent: " .. v.Parent.Name)
                end
            end
            task.wait(5) -- Print every 5 seconds
        end
    end)
end

local function StopPartViewer()
    PartViewerEnabled = false
    SendNotification("Part Viewer stopped", 3)
end

-- === EXTERNAL HELPER FUNCTIONS (To reduce StartCheat locals) ===

local function RandomNumberRange(a)
    return math.random(-a * 100, a * 100) / 100
end

local function ApplyDescriptionCustom(humanoid, description)
    local character = humanoid.Parent
    if not character then return end
    
    -- 1. Body Colors
    local bodyColors = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyColors")
    if not bodyColors then
        bodyColors = Instance.new("BodyColors")
        bodyColors.Name = "Body Colors"
        bodyColors.Parent = character
    end
    bodyColors.HeadColor3 = description.HeadColor
    bodyColors.TorsoColor3 = description.TorsoColor
    bodyColors.LeftArmColor3 = description.LeftArmColor
    bodyColors.RightArmColor3 = description.RightArmColor
    bodyColors.LeftLegColor3 = description.LeftLegColor
    bodyColors.RightLegColor3 = description.RightLegColor
    
    -- 2. Clothing
    local function updateClothing(className, propName, id)
        if id and id > 0 then
            task.spawn(function()
                local success, result = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. id) end)
                if success and result then
                    for _, obj in pairs(result) do
                        if obj:IsA(className) then
                            local item = character:FindFirstChildOfClass(className)
                            if not item then
                                item = Instance.new(className)
                                item.Parent = character
                            end
                            item[propName] = obj[propName]
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end)
        else
            local item = character:FindFirstChildOfClass(className)
            if item then item:Destroy() end
        end
    end
    
    updateClothing("Shirt", "ShirtTemplate", description.Shirt)
    updateClothing("Pants", "PantsTemplate", description.Pants)
    updateClothing("ShirtGraphic", "Graphic", description.GraphicTShirt)
    
    -- 3. Face
    local head = character:FindFirstChild("Head")
    if head then
        local face = head:FindFirstChildOfClass("Decal")
        if description.Face and description.Face > 0 then
            if not face then
                face = Instance.new("Decal")
                face.Name = "face"
                face.Parent = head
            end
            face.Texture = "rbxassetid://" .. description.Face
        else
            if face then face:Destroy() end
        end
    end
    
    -- 4. Accessories
    for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if v:IsA("Accessory") then v:Destroy() end
    end
    
    local function loadAccessories(ids)
        if not ids or ids == "" then return end
        for id in string.gmatch(ids, "([^,]+)") do
            local assetId = tonumber(id)
            if assetId then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local success, result = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. assetId) end)
                    if success and result then
                        for _, obj in pairs(result) do
                            if obj:IsA("Accessory") then obj.Parent = character end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
    
    loadAccessories(description.HatAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.HairAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.FaceAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.NeckAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.ShouldersAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.FrontAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.BackAccessory)
    loadAccessories(description.WaistAccessory)
    
    -- 5. Body Parts (R6 & R15)
    for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if v:IsA("CharacterMesh") then v:Destroy() end
    end
    
    local function loadBodyParts(id)
        if not id or id == 0 then return end
        task.spawn(function()
            local success, result = pcall(function() return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. id) end)
            if success and result then
                for _, obj in pairs(result) do
                    local function recurse(item)
                        if item:IsA("CharacterMesh") then
                            item.Parent = character
                        elseif item:IsA("MeshPart") and humanoid.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.R15 then
                            local charPart = character:FindFirstChild(item.Name)
                            if charPart and charPart:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                pcall(function() charPart.MeshId = item.MeshId end)
                                pcall(function() charPart.TextureID = item.TextureID end)
                                pcall(function() charPart.Size = item.Size end)
                            end
                        end
                        for _, child in pairs(item:GetChildren()) do
                            recurse(child)
                        end
                    end
                    recurse(obj)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    
    loadBodyParts(description.Head)
    loadBodyParts(description.Torso)
    loadBodyParts(description.LeftArm)
    loadBodyParts(description.RightArm)
    loadBodyParts(description.LeftLeg)
    loadBodyParts(description.RightLeg)
    
    -- 6. Scales
    local function updateScale(name, val)
        if not val then return end
        local valObj = humanoid:FindFirstChild(name)
        if not valObj then
            valObj = Instance.new("NumberValue")
            valObj.Name = name
            valObj.Parent = humanoid
        end
        valObj.Value = val
    end
    
    updateScale("BodyHeightScale", description.HeightScale)
    updateScale("BodyWidthScale", description.WidthScale)
    updateScale("BodyDepthScale", description.DepthScale)
    updateScale("HeadScale", description.HeadScale)
    updateScale("BodyProportionScale", description.ProportionScale)
    updateScale("BodyTypeScale", description.BodyTypeScale)
end

local function disableDamageBlock(part)
    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
        local name = part.Name:lower()
        local parentName = part.Parent and part.Parent.Name:lower() or ""
        local shouldDisable = false
        
        -- Detect Damage Zones (Expanded Keywords + Parent Check)
        local damageKeywords = {"lava", "magma", "acid", "water", "damage", "burn", "kill", "death", "hurt", "void", "spike", "fire", "flame", "trap", "laser"}
        for _, kw in pairs(damageKeywords) do
            if (string.find(name, kw) or string.find(parentName, kw)) and not string.find(name, "safe") and not string.find(name, "spawn") then
                shouldDisable = true
                break
            end
        end
        
        if part.Material == Enum.Material.CrackedLava or part.Material == Enum.Material.Water then shouldDisable = true end
        
        -- Check Children (Textures/Decals) as requested by user
        if not shouldDisable then
            for _, child in pairs(part:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("Texture") or child:IsA("Decal") then
                    local texName = child.Name:lower()
                    for _, kw in pairs(damageKeywords) do
                        if string.find(texName, kw) then shouldDisable = true break end
                    end
                end
                if shouldDisable then break end
            end
        end
        
        if shouldDisable then
            pcall(function()
                part.CanTouch = false
                part.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic -- Bypass FloorMaterial checks
                part.Name = "SafeZone_Bypassed" -- Bypass Name checks
                if part:FindFirstChildOfClass("TouchInterest") then
                    part:FindFirstChildOfClass("TouchInterest"):Destroy()
                end
            end)
        end
    end
end

    -- === WEAPON EXTENDER / SKIN GLITCH FUNCTIONS (Moved Up) ===
    local function SetWeaponSize(multiplier)
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        
        for _, tool in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
            if tool:IsA("Tool") then
                local handle = tool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
                if handle and handle:IsA("BasePart") then
                    local compensationMultiplier = multiplier
                    if Config.SizeMultiplierEnabled then
                        compensationMultiplier = multiplier * Config.SizeMultiplier
                    end
                    
                    if not originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name] then
                        originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name] = {}
                        originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name].HandleSize = handle.Size
                    end
                    
                    handle.Size = originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name].HandleSize * compensationMultiplier
                    handle.CanCollide = false
                    handle.Massless = true
                    handle.Transparency = Config.WeaponTransparency
                end
                
                for _, part in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
                    pcall(function()
                        if part:IsA("BasePart") and part ~= handle then
                            local compensationMultiplier = multiplier
                            if Config.SizeMultiplierEnabled then
                                compensationMultiplier = multiplier * Config.SizeMultiplier
                            end
                            
                            if not originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name] then
                                originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name] = part.Size
                            end
                            part.Size = originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name] * compensationMultiplier
                            part.CanCollide = false
                            part.Massless = true
                            part.Transparency = Config.WeaponTransparency
                            
                        elseif part:IsA("Attachment") then
                            local compensationMultiplier = multiplier
                            if Config.SizeMultiplierEnabled then
                                compensationMultiplier = multiplier * Config.SizeMultiplier
                            end
                            
                            if not originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Pos"] then
                                originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Pos"] = part.Position
                            end
                            part.Position = originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Pos"] * compensationMultiplier
                            
                        elseif part:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                            local compensationMultiplier = multiplier
                            if Config.SizeMultiplierEnabled then
                                compensationMultiplier = multiplier * Config.SizeMultiplier
                            end
                            
                            if not originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Scale"] then
                                originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Scale"] = part.Scale
                            end
                            part.Scale = originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name][part.Name .. "_Scale"] * compensationMultiplier
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end

        -- Enlarge hands
        local leftHand = character:FindFirstChild("LeftHand") or character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("LeftArm")
        local rightHand = character:FindFirstChild("RightHand") or character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("RightArm")
        if leftHand and leftHand:IsA("BasePart") then
            if not originalHandSizes["Left"] then originalHandSizes["Left"] = leftHand.Size end
            leftHand.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 2) * multiplier -- Enlarge hands
            leftHand.Transparency = Config.WeaponTransparency
        end
        if rightHand and rightHand:IsA("BasePart") then
            if not originalHandSizes["Right"] then originalHandSizes["Right"] = rightHand.Size end
            rightHand.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 2) * multiplier -- Enlarge hands
            rightHand.Transparency = Config.WeaponTransparency
        end
    end

    local function RestoreWeaponSize()
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        
        -- Restore Tools
        for toolName, data in pairs(originalWeaponSizes) do
            local tool = character:FindFirstChild(toolName) or player.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName)
            if tool then
                local handle = tool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
                if handle and data.HandleSize then
                    handle.Size = data.HandleSize
                    handle.Transparency = 0
                end
                for partName, size in pairs(data) do
                    if type(size) == "Vector3" and partName ~= "HandleSize" then
                         for _, p in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
                             if p.Name == partName and p:IsA("BasePart") then
                                 p.Size = size
                                 p.Transparency = 0
                             end
                         end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Restore Hands
        local leftHand = character:FindFirstChild("LeftHand") or character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("LeftArm")
        local rightHand = character:FindFirstChild("RightHand") or character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or character:FindFirstChild("RightArm")
        if leftHand and leftHand:IsA("BasePart") and originalHandSizes["Left"] then
            leftHand.Size = originalHandSizes["Left"]
            leftHand.Transparency = 0
        end
        if rightHand and rightHand:IsA("BasePart") and originalHandSizes["Right"] then
            rightHand.Size = originalHandSizes["Right"]
            rightHand.Transparency = 0
        end
    end

    local function WatchForNewTools()
        local character = player.Character
        if not character then return end
        
        table.insert(Connections, character.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
            if child:IsA("Tool") and Config.WeaponExtender then
                task.wait(0.2)
                SetWeaponSize(Config.WeaponLength)
            end
        end))
        
        table.insert(Connections, player.Backpack.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
            if child:IsA("Tool") and Config.WeaponExtender then
                task.wait(0.2)
                SetWeaponSize(Config.WeaponLength)
            end
        end))
    end

    -- === HELPER FUNCTIONS ===
    
    getClosestPlayerToMouse = function(fovRadius, useFilter)
        local closestPlayer = nil
        
        -- Fix Hitbox Extender: Augmente le FOV pour dÃ©tecter les clics sur les bords des hitboxes gÃ©antes
        local effectiveFOV = fovRadius
        if Config.HitboxExpander then effectiveFOV = 2000 end 
        
        local shortestDistance = effectiveFOV or math.huge
        local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()

        for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local targetPart = p.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                
                -- Aim Filter Check
                local allow = true
                if Config.TeamCheck and p.Team and player.Team and p.Team == player.Team then allow = false end
                if useFilter and Config.AimFilter then
                    local status = Config.AimFilterList[p.Name]
                    if Config.AimFilterMode == "Whitelist" then
                        if not Config.AimFilterWhitelist[p.Name] then allow = false end
                        if status ~= "Whitelist" then allow = false end
                    elseif Config.AimFilterMode == "Blacklist" then
                        if Config.AimFilterBlacklist[p.Name] then allow = false end
                        if status == "Blacklist" then allow = false end
                    end
                end
                
                if targetPart and allow then
                    local isInRange = true
                    if rootPart and Config.SilentRange > 0 then
                        local dist = (rootPart.Position - targetPart.Position).Magnitude
                        if dist > Config.SilentRange then isInRange = false end
                    end
                    
                    if isInRange then
                        local pos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(targetPart.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            local distance = (Vector2.new(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y) - Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)).Magnitude
                            if distance < shortestDistance then
                                closestPlayer = p
                                shortestDistance = distance
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        return closestPlayer
    end
    
    -- Cible TOUT (NPC + Joueurs)
    local function getClosestEnemy(range)
        local closest = nil
        local dist = range
        
        -- Scan Workspace Children (NPCs)
        for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
            if obj ~= character and obj:IsA("Model") then
                local hum = obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                local root = obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                
                if hum and root and hum.Health > 0 then
                    local mag = (rootPart.Position - root.Position).Magnitude
                    if mag < dist then
                        closest = obj
                        dist = mag
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Scan Players
        for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local mag = (rootPart.Position - p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                if mag < dist then
                    closest = p.Character
                    dist = mag
                end
            end
        end
        
        return closest
    end
    
    local function getClosestTargetToMouse(fovRadius)
        local closest = nil
        local minDist = fovRadius or math.huge
        local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
        
        -- Check Players
        for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local root = p.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                local pos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(root.Position)
                if onScreen then
                    local dist = (Vector2.new(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y) - Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)).Magnitude
                    if dist < minDist then
                        closest = p.Character
                        minDist = dist
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Check NPCs
        for _, obj in pairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
            if obj:IsA("Model") and obj ~= character and obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and obj.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local root = obj.HumanoidRootPart
                local pos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(root.Position)
                if onScreen then
                    local dist = (Vector2.new(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y) - Vector2.new(pos.X, pos.Y)).Magnitude
                    if dist < minDist then
                        closest = obj
                        minDist = dist
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        return closest
    end

    local function getColorAt(x, y)
        -- 1. Priority: getcolor (Reads screen pixels including UI/GUI)
        if getcolor then
            return getcolor(Vector2.new(x, y))
        end
        -- 2. Fallback: Raycast (3D World only - Cannot see UI)
        local inset = GuiService:GetGuiInset()
        local ray = camera:ViewportPointToRay(x, y - inset.Y)
        
        local params = RaycastParams.new()
        params.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude
        params.FilterDescendantsInstances = {character, ESPFolder, camera}
        
        local res = workspace:Raycast(ray.Origin, ray.Direction * 1000, params)
        if res and res.Instance and res.Instance:IsA("BasePart") then
            return res.Instance.Color
        end
        return Color3.new(0,0,0)
    end

    local function applyToolColor(obj)
        if not Config.ToolColorChanger then return end
        pcall(function()
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", obj.Color)
                end
                obj.Color = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or obj:IsA("Trail") or obj:IsA("Beam") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColorSequence") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColorSequence", obj.Color)
                end
                obj.Color = ColorSequence.new(Config.ToolColor)
            elseif obj:IsA("Light") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalLightColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalLightColor", obj.Color)
                end
                obj.Color = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("Fire") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", obj.Color)
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalSecondaryColor", obj.SecondaryColor)
                end
                obj.Color = Config.ToolColor
                obj.SecondaryColor = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("Smoke") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", obj.Color)
                end
                obj.Color = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("Sparkles") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", obj.SparkleColor)
                end
                obj.SparkleColor = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("Decal") or obj:IsA("Texture") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", obj.Color3)
                end
                obj.Color3 = Config.ToolColor
            elseif obj:IsA("SelectionBox") or obj:IsA("SelectionSphere") or obj:IsA("Highlight") then
                if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalColor") then
                    local color = (obj:IsA("Highlight") and obj.FillColor) or obj.Color
                    obj:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", color)
                end
                if obj:IsA("Highlight") then
                    obj.FillColor = Config.ToolColor
                    obj.OutlineColor = Config.ToolColor
                else
                    obj.Color = Config.ToolColor
                end
            end
        end)
    end

    local vfxClasses = {
        ["ParticleEmitter"] = true, ["Trail"] = true, ["Beam"] = true, 
        ["Fire"] = true, ["Smoke"] = true, ["Sparkles"] = true,
        ["Explosion"] = true, ["PointLight"] = true, 
        ["SpotLight"] = true, ["SurfaceLight"] = true,
        ["BloomEffect"] = true, ["BlurEffect"] = true,

        ["Sky"] = true

    local function makePotato(obj)
        pcall(function()
            local nameLower = obj.Name:lower()
            if vfxClasses[obj.ClassName] or nameLower:find("aura") or nameLower:find("effect") or nameLower:find("glow") then
                if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                    obj.Transparency = Config.PotatoGraphics and 1 or 0
                else
                    obj.Enabled = not Config.PotatoGraphics
                end
            end
            
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
                if Config.PotatoGraphics then
                    if not obj:GetAttribute("OriginalMaterial") then
                        obj:SetAttribute("OriginalMaterial", obj.Material)
                    end
                    obj.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
                    obj.CastShadow = false
                    obj.Reflectance = 0
                else
                    local original = obj:GetAttribute("OriginalMaterial")
                    if original then obj.Material = original end
                    obj.CastShadow = true
                end
            end

            if obj:IsA("MeshPart") or obj:IsA("SpecialMesh") then
                if Config.PotatoGraphics then
                    if obj:IsA("MeshPart") then
                        obj.RenderFidelity = Enum.RenderFidelity.Performance
                    end
                end
            end

            if obj:IsA("Decal") or obj:IsA("Texture") then
                obj.Transparency = Config.PotatoGraphics and 1 or 0
            end
        end)
    end
    
    -- === SILENT AIM HOOK (Streamable) ===
    local __index
    local __namecall
    
    pcall(function()
        -- Global Wait Hooks for No Cooldown
        local oldWait = wait
        getgenv().wait = function(n)
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                return oldWait()
            end
            return oldWait(n)
        end
        
        local oldTaskWait = task.wait
        getgenv().task.wait = function(n)
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                return oldTaskWait()
            end
            return oldTaskWait(n)
        end

        -- Time Hooks to bypass "tick() - lastUse" checks
        local oldTick = tick
        getgenv().tick = function()
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                return oldTick() + 9e9
            end
            return oldTick()
        end

        local oldOsClock = os.clock
        getgenv().os.clock = function()
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                return oldOsClock() + 9e9
            end
            return oldOsClock()
        end

        local oldOsTime = os.time
        getgenv().os.time = function()
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                return oldOsTime() + 9e9
            end
            return oldOsTime()
        end

        -- Low-level HookFunction for Time (Unbypassable by localization)
        if hookfunction then
            local oldT; oldT = hookfunction(tick, function()
                if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then return oldT() + 9e9 end
                return oldT()
            end)
            local oldC; oldC = hookfunction(os.clock, function()
                if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then return oldC() + 9e9 end
                return oldC()
            end)
        end

        __index = hookmetamethod(game, "__index", function(t, k)
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                local tStr = tostring(t):lower()
                local kStr = tostring(k):lower()
                
                -- Catch all cooldown-related value reads
                if (kStr == "value" or kStr == "Value") then
                    local name = ""
                    pcall(function() name = t.Name:lower() end)
                    if name:find("cooldown") or name:find("cd") or name:find("skill") or name:find("timer") or name:find("ability") or name:find("stun") or name:find("busy") then
                        return 0
                    end
                end
                
                -- Catch cooldown property reads
                if kStr:find("cooldown") or kStr == "cd" or kStr == "skillcd" then
                    return 0
                end
                
                -- Catch stun/busy states
                if kStr == "stun" or kStr == "busy" or kStr == "using" or kStr == "casting" or kStr == "attacking" then
                    return false
                end
            end

            -- Fix: Active le Silent Aim automatiquement si Hitbox Extender est ON pour valider les dÃ©gÃ¢ts serveur
            if (Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander or Config.CursorLock) and (t == mouse or tostring(t) == "Mouse") then
                if k == "Hit" or k == "Target" or k == "UnitRay" then
                    local targetChar = nil
                    if Config.CursorLock and cursorLockTarget then
                        targetChar = cursorLockTarget
                    elseif Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander then
                        local p = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                        if p then targetChar = p.Character end
                    end
                    if targetChar then
                        -- PrioritÃ© au Torse (HumanoidRootPart) car plus gros
                        local targetPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Torso") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            if k == "Hit" then return targetPart.CFrame end
                            if k == "Target" then return targetPart end
                            if k == "UnitRay" then 
                                local origin = camera.CFrame.Position
                                local direction = (targetPart.Position - origin).Unit
                                return Ray.new(origin, direction)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return __index(t, k)
        end)
        
        __namecall = hookmetamethod(game, "__namecall", function(self, ...)
            local method = getnamecallmethod()
            local args = {...}
            
            if Config.NoCooldown and not checkcaller() then
                if method == "GetAttribute" then
                    local attr = args[1]
                    if type(attr) == "string" then
                        local attrL = attr:lower()
                        if attrL:find("cooldown") or attrL:find("cd") or attrL:find("lastuse") or attrL:find("nextuse") or attrL:find("timer") then
                            return 0
                        end
                        if attrL == "stun" or attrL == "busy" or attrL == "using" or attrL == "casting" or attrL == "attacking" then
                            return false
                        end
                    end
                elseif method == "InvokeServer" or method == "FireServer" then
                    -- Block/Modify only cooldown-setting remotes
                    local selfName = tostring(self):lower()
                    if selfName == "commf_" or selfName:find("remote") or selfName:find("event") then
                        local cmd = args[1]
                        if type(cmd) == "string" then
                            local cmdLower = cmd:lower()
                            if cmdLower == "cooldown" or cmdLower == "setcooldown" or cmdLower:find("skillcooldown") or cmdLower:find("abilitycooldown") then
                                return nil
                            end
                        end
                    end
                elseif method == "SetAttribute" then
                    local attr = args[1]
                    if type(attr) == "string" then
                        local attrL = attr:lower()
                        if attrL:find("cooldown") or attrL:find("cd") or attrL == "stun" or attrL == "busy" or attrL == "using" or attrL == "casting" or attrL == "attacking" then
                            return
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            if (Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander or Config.CursorLock) and method == "GetMouseLocation" then
                local targetChar = nil
                if Config.CursorLock and cursorLockTarget then
                    targetChar = cursorLockTarget
                elseif Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander then
                    local p = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                    if p then targetChar = p.Character end
                end
                if targetChar then
                    local targetPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Torso") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if targetPart then
                        local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(targetPart.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            return Vector2.new(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            if (Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander or Config.CursorLock) then
                if method == "Raycast" and self == workspace then
                    local targetChar = nil
                    if Config.CursorLock and cursorLockTarget then
                        targetChar = cursorLockTarget
                    elseif Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander then
                        local p = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                        if p then targetChar = p.Character end
                    end
                    if targetChar then
                        local targetPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Torso") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local origin = args[1]
                            local direction = (targetPart.Position - origin).Unit * args[2].Magnitude
                            return __namecall(self, origin, direction, args[3])
                        end
                    end
                elseif (method == "ScreenPointToRay" or method == "ViewportPointToRay") and self == camera then
                    local targetChar = nil
                    if Config.CursorLock and cursorLockTarget then
                        targetChar = cursorLockTarget
                    elseif Config.SilentAim or Config.HitboxExpander then
                        local p = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                        if p then targetChar = p.Character end
                    end
                    if targetChar then
                        local targetPart = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Torso") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local origin = self.CFrame.Position
                            local direction = (targetPart.Position - origin).Unit
                            return Ray.new(origin, direction)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return __namecall(self, ...)
        end)
    end)
    
    
    -- Helper to check if any combat key is currently held down
    local function IsCombatKeyDown()
        -- Check Keyboard Keys
        for _, key in pairs(Config.CombatKeys) do
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(key) then
                return true
            end
        end
        -- Check Mouse
        return false
    end

    -- GOD MODE CLICK FUNCTION (BURST SPAM)
    local function NuclearClick(targetOverride)
        local clickX, clickY
        local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
        
        if targetOverride then
            clickX = targetOverride.X
            clickY = targetOverride.Y
        else
            clickX = mousePos.X
            clickY = mousePos.Y
        end
        
        -- Prevent clicking on Cheat GUI
        local gui = CoreGui:FindFirstChild("DesyncGUI_V102") or (player.PlayerGui and player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("DesyncGUI_V102"))
        if gui then
            local mainFrame = gui:FindFirstChild("MainFrame")
            if mainFrame and mainFrame.Visible then
                local absPos = mainFrame.AbsolutePosition
                local absSize = mainFrame.AbsoluteSize
                if clickX >= absPos.X and clickX <= absPos.X + absSize.X and clickY >= absPos.Y and clickY <= absPos.Y + absSize.Y then return end
            end
        end
        
        -- Force Mouse Move Instant
        pcall(function()
            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseMoveEvent(clickX, clickY, game)
        end)
        
        -- Click
        pcall(function()
            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(clickX, clickY, 0, true, game, 1)
            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(clickX, clickY, 0, false, game, 1)
        end)
        if mouse1click then mouse1click() end
        
        if character then
            local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
            if tool and (Config.EasyLock or tick() - lastToolUse > 0.25) then
                tool:Activate()
                lastToolUse = tick()
            end
        end
    end
    
    local function ClearESP()
        ESPFolder:ClearAllChildren()
    end

    -- Bind Instant Respawn to Humanoid.Died
    local function BindInstantRespawn()
        if instantRespawnConn then instantRespawnConn:Disconnect(); instantRespawnConn = nil end
        if character then
            local hum = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            if hum then
                instantRespawnConn = hum.Died:Connect(function()
                    task.defer(function()
                        pcall(function() player:LoadCharacter() end)
                    end)
                end)
            end
        end
    end



    local function UpdateESP()
        if not Config.ESPBox and not Config.ESPName and not Config.ESPLvl and not Config.ESPHP and not Config.ESPChams and not Config.ESPDot and not Config.ESPNPC and not Config.ESPFruit and not Config.ShowMoney and not Config.ShowFragments and not Config.ShowBounty and not Config.ESPTracers and not Config.ESPPlayerDistance and not Config.ESPIsland then
            ClearESP()
            return
        end

        for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                local char = p.Character
                local root = char.HumanoidRootPart
                local hum = char.Humanoid
                
                local espId = p.Name .. "_ESP"
                local espGroup = ESPFolder:FindFirstChild(espId)
                
                if not espGroup then
                    espGroup = Instance.new("Folder")
                    espGroup.Name = espId
                    espGroup.Parent = ESPFolder
                    
                    -- Box
                    local box = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
                    box.Name = "Box"
                    box.Adornee = root
                    box.LineThickness = 0.05
                    box.Parent = espGroup

                    -- Text Info
                    local bb = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
                    bb.Name = "Info"
                    bb.Adornee = char:FindFirstChild("Head") or root
                    bb.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 50)
                    bb.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3.5, 0)
                    bb.AlwaysOnTop = true
                    bb.MaxDistance = math.huge
                    bb.Parent = espGroup
                    
                    local txt = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                    txt.Name = "ESPText"
                    txt.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                    txt.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                    txt.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
                    txt.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0,0,0)
                    txt.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    txt.TextSize = 12
                    txt.Text = ""
                    txt.RichText = false
                    txt.Parent = bb
                end
                
                if espGroup then
                    local box = espGroup:FindFirstChild("Box")
                    local bb = espGroup:FindFirstChild("Info")
                    
                    -- WALL HACK (CHAMS) LOGIC
                    local highlight = char:FindFirstChild("CyberChams")
                    if Config.ESPChams then
                        if not highlight then
                            highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
                            highlight.Name = "CyberChams"
                            highlight.Parent = char
                            highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
                            highlight.FillColor = CurrentThemeColor
                            highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                            highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
                            highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
                        end
                    else
                        if highlight then highlight:Destroy() end
                    end
                    
                    -- DOT LOGIC (RED POINT)
                    local dotGui = espGroup:FindFirstChild("DotGui")
                    if Config.ESPDot then
                        if not dotGui then
                            dotGui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
                            dotGui.Name = "DotGui"
                            dotGui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
                            dotGui.AlwaysOnTop = true
                            dotGui.Adornee = root
                            dotGui.Parent = espGroup
                            
                            local dotFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                            dotFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                            dotFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0) -- Red
                            dotFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                            dotFrame.Parent = dotGui
                            
                            local dotCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
                            dotCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0) -- Circle
                            dotCorner.Parent = dotFrame
                        end
                        dotGui.Enabled = true
                    else
                        if dotGui then dotGui:Destroy() end
                    end
                    
                    local hpPercent = hum.Health / hum.MaxHealth
                    local customColor = Color3.fromRGB(Config.ESPColorR, Config.ESPColorG, Config.ESPColorB)
                    local useColor = customColor
                    
                    -- TRACERS LOGIC (LINES)
                    local targetAtt = root:FindFirstChild("ESP_Target_Att")
                    if not targetAtt then targetAtt = Instance.new("Attachment"); targetAtt.Name = "ESP_Target_Att"; targetAtt.Parent = root end
                    
                    local beam = targetAtt:FindFirstChild("TracerBeam")
                    
                    if Config.ESPTracers then
                        local myRoot = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if myRoot then
                            local myAtt = myRoot:FindFirstChild("ESP_Origin_Att")
                            if not myAtt then
                                myAtt = Instance.new("Attachment")
                                myAtt.Name = "ESP_Origin_Att"
                                myAtt.Parent = myRoot
                            end
                            
                            if not beam then
                                beam = Instance.new("Beam")
                                beam.Name = "TracerBeam"
                                beam.FaceCamera = true
                                beam.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
                                beam.Width0 = 0.1
                                beam.Width1 = 0.1
                                beam.Parent = targetAtt -- Fix: Parent to Workspace to be visible
                            end
                            
                            beam.Attachment0 = myAtt
                            beam.Attachment1 = targetAtt
                            beam.Color = ColorSequence.new(useColor)
                            beam.Enabled = true
                        end
                    else
                        if beam then beam:Destroy() end
                    end
                    
                    if box then
                        if Config.ESPBox then
                            box.Visible = true
                            box.Adornee = root
                            box.Color3 = useColor
                        else
                            box.Visible = false
                        end
                    end
                    
                    if bb and bb:FindFirstChild("ESPText") then
                        local txtLabel = bb.ESPText
                        if Config.ESPName or Config.ESPHP or Config.ESPLvl or Config.ESPPlayerDistance or Config.ESPIsland or (Config.InspectorName ~= "" and (Config.ShowMoney or Config.ShowFragments or Config.ShowBounty) and string.find(p.Name:lower(), Config.InspectorName:lower())) then
                            bb.Enabled = true
                            bb.Adornee = char:FindFirstChild("Head") or root
                            
                            local textStr = ""
                            if Config.ESPName then textStr = textStr .. p.Name end
                            if Config.ESPLvl then
                                local lvl = 0
                                pcall(function() lvl = p.Data.Level.Value end)
                                if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                textStr = textStr .. "[Lv. " .. lvl .. "]"
                            end
                            if Config.ESPHP then
                                if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                textStr = textStr .. "[" .. math.floor(hum.Health) .. " HP]"
                            end
                            
                            -- Player Distance
                            if Config.ESPPlayerDistance then
                                local myRoot = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if myRoot and root then
                                    local dist = (root.Position - myRoot.Position).Magnitude
                                    local distMeters = math.floor(dist * 0.4) -- Convert studs to approximate meters
                                    if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                    textStr = textStr .. "[" .. distMeters .. "m]"
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Island
                            if Config.ESPIsland then
                                local locationAttr = p:GetAttribute("CurrentLocation")
                                if locationAttr ~= nil and locationAttr ~= "" then
                                    if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                    textStr = textStr .. "[" .. tostring(locationAttr) .. "]"
                                end
                            end
                            
                            if Config.InspectorName ~= "" and string.find(p.Name:lower(), Config.InspectorName:lower()) then
                                if Config.ShowMoney then
                                    local val = 0
                                    pcall(function() val = p.Data.Beli.Value end)
                                    if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                    textStr = textStr .. "[ðŸ’° " .. val .. "]"
                                end
                                if Config.ShowFragments then
                                    local val = 0
                                    pcall(function() val = p.Data.Fragments.Value end)
                                    if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                    textStr = textStr .. "[ðŸŸ£ " .. val .. "]"
                                end
                                if Config.ShowBounty then
                                    local val = 0
                                    pcall(function() val = p.leaderstats["Bounty/Honor"].Value end)
                                    if textStr ~= "" then textStr = textStr .. "\n" end
                                    textStr = textStr .. "[ðŸ›¡ï¸ " .. val .. "]"
                                end
                            end
                            
                            txtLabel.Text = textStr
                            txtLabel.TextColor3 = useColor
                            txtLabel.TextSize = Config.ESPSize
                        else
                            bb.Enabled = false
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                local espGroup = ESPFolder:FindFirstChild(p.Name .. "_ESP")
                if espGroup then espGroup:Destroy() end
            end
        end

        -- NPC ESP LOOP
        if Config.ESPNPC then
            local function processNPC(model)
                if model ~= character and model:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and model:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and model.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    if Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(model) then return end
                    
                    local espId = "_NPC_" .. tostring(model) .. "_" .. model:GetDebugId()
                    local espGroup = ESPFolder:FindFirstChild(espId)
                    
                    if not espGroup then
                        espGroup = Instance.new("Folder")
                        espGroup.Name = espId
                        espGroup.Parent = ESPFolder
                        
                        local box = Instance.new("BoxHandleAdornment")
                        box.Name = "Box"
                        box.Size = Vector3.new(4, 5, 1)
                        box.Adornee = model.HumanoidRootPart
                        box.AlwaysOnTop = true
                        box.ZIndex = 5
                        box.Transparency = 0.6
                        box.Color3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 150, 0)
                        box.Parent = espGroup
                        
                        local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
                        highlight.Name = "NPCChams"
                        highlight.Parent = model
                        highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
                        highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 150, 0)
                        highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                        highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
                        highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
                        
                        local href = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
                        href.Name = "HighlightRef"
                        href.Value = highlight
                        href.Parent = espGroup
                    end
                end
            end
            
            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("Model") then processNPC(v) end end
            if workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies") then for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("Model") then processNPC(v) end end end
        end
        
        for _, child in pairs(ESPFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if child.Name:sub(1, 5) == "_NPC_" then
                local box = child:FindFirstChild("Box")
                if not Config.ESPNPC or not box or not box.Adornee or not box.Adornee.Parent or box.Adornee.Parent.Humanoid.Health <= 0 then
                    local href = child:FindFirstChild("HighlightRef")
                    if href and href.Value then href.Value:Destroy() end
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            else
                local playerName = child.Name:gsub("_ESP", "")
                if not Players:FindFirstChild(playerName) then
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- FRUIT ESP LOOP
    if Config.ESPFruit then
        local detectedFruits = {}
        
        -- Scan entire workspace for fruits (Dough Fruit and other fruits)
        for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if v:IsA("Tool") and (v.Name == "Dough Fruit" or v.ToolTip == "Blox Fruit" or v.Name:find("Fruit")) then
                local handle = v:FindFirstChild("Handle")
                if handle then
                    local espId = "_FRUIT_" .. tostring(handle)
                    table.insert(detectedFruits, {id = espId, handle = handle})
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Create ESP for all detected fruits
        for _, fruitData in pairs(detectedFruits) do
            local espGroup = ESPFolder:FindFirstChild(fruitData.id)
            
            if not espGroup then
                espGroup = Instance.new("Folder")
                espGroup.Name = fruitData.id
                espGroup.Parent = ESPFolder
                
                -- RED AURA (using Highlight)
                local highlight = Instance.new("Highlight")
                highlight.Name = "FruitHighlight"
                highlight.Adornee = fruitData.handle
                highlight.DepthMode = Enum.HighlightDepthMode.AlwaysOnTop
                highlight.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                highlight.FillTransparency = 0.5
                highlight.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                highlight.OutlineTransparency = 0
                highlight.Parent = espGroup
                
                -- "Fruit" text tag
                local bb = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
                bb.Name = "FruitInfo"
                bb.Adornee = fruitData.handle
                bb.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 30)
                bb.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                bb.AlwaysOnTop = true
                bb.MaxDistance = 3000
                bb.Parent = espGroup
                
                local txt = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                txt.Name = "FruitText"
                txt.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                txt.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                txt.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
                txt.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
                txt.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                txt.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                txt.TextSize = 18
                txt.Text = "Fruit"
                txt.RichText = false
                txt.Parent = bb
                
                local href = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
                href.Name = "HighlightRef"
                href.Value = highlight
                href.Parent = espGroup
            end
        end
        
        -- Cleanup old fruit ESP
        for _, child in pairs(ESPFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if child.Name:sub(1, 8) == "_FRUIT_" then
                local highlightRef = child:FindFirstChild("HighlightRef")
                local found = false
                
                for _, fruitData in pairs(detectedFruits) do
                    if fruitData.id == child.Name then
                        found = true
                        break
                    end
                end
                
                if not found then
                    if highlightRef and highlightRef.Value then highlightRef.Value:Destroy() end
                    child:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end
    else
        -- Cleanup all fruit ESP if disabled
        for _, child in pairs(ESPFolder:GetChildren()) do
            if child.Name:sub(1, 8) == "_FRUIT_" then
                local highlightRef = child:FindFirstChild("HighlightRef")
                if highlightRef and highlightRef.Value then highlightRef.Value:Destroy() end
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- ==================================================================
    --                          MAIN GUI (Professional)
    -- ==================================================================

    local CurrentThemeColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)

    -- Cleanup existing GUI and Sound to prevent duplicates
    if CoreGui:FindFirstChild("DesyncGUI_V102") then CoreGui.DesyncGUI_V102:Destroy() end
    if player.PlayerGui and player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("DesyncGUI_V102") then player.PlayerGui.DesyncGUI_V102:Destroy() end

    local ScreenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    ScreenGui.Name = "DesyncGUI_V102"
    pcall(function() ScreenGui.Parent = CoreGui end)
    if not ScreenGui.Parent then ScreenGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui") end

    local MainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    MainFrame.Name = "MainFrame"
    MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 400, 0, 500) 
    MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -200, 0.5, -250)
    MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 15, 20)
    MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    MainFrame.Active = true
    MainFrame.Draggable = false
    MainFrame.ClipsDescendants = true -- Important pour l'animation
    MainFrame.Parent = ScreenGui

    local MainStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
    MainStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
    MainStroke.Thickness = 1
    MainStroke.Parent = MainFrame

    local UICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
    UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
    UICorner.Parent = MainFrame

    -- === STATS GUI (Top Left) ===
    local StatsFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
    StatsFrame.Name = "StatsFrame"
    StatsFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 100)
    StatsFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
    StatsFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    StatsFrame.Parent = ScreenGui
    
    local StatsLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
    StatsLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
    StatsLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 2)
    StatsLayout.Parent = StatsFrame
    
    local function createStatLabel(name)
        local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        label.Name = name
        label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 15)
        label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        label.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        label.TextSize = 12
        label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
        label.Visible = false
        label.Parent = StatsFrame
        return label
    end
    
    local FPSLabel = createStatLabel("FPSLabel")
    local PingLabel = createStatLabel("PingLabel")
    local UptimeLabel = createStatLabel("UptimeLabel")
    local ServerLabel = createStatLabel("ServerLabel")
    
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            pcall(function()
                if ScreenGui and StatsFrame then
                    FPSLabel.Visible = Config.ShowFPS
                    FPSLabel.Text = "FPS: " .. math.floor(workspace:GetRealPhysicsFPS())
                    FPSLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    
                    PingLabel.Visible = Config.ShowPing
                    PingLabel.Text = "Ping: " .. math.floor(game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValue()) .. " ms"
                    PingLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    
                    UptimeLabel.Visible = Config.ShowUptime
                    local t = workspace.DistributedGameTime
                    local hours = math.floor(t / 3600)
                    local mins = math.floor((t % 3600) / 60)
                    local secs = math.floor(t % 60)
                    UptimeLabel.Text = string.format("Server Time: %02d:%02d:%02d", hours, mins, secs)
                    UptimeLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    
                    ServerLabel.Visible = Config.ShowServer
                    ServerLabel.Text = "Region: " .. cachedRegion
                    ServerLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                end
            end)
            task.wait(1)
        end
    end)

    -- === MINIMIZE SYSTEM ===
    local isMinimized = false
local MinimizedGui = nil
local dragConnection = nil

local function restoreGui()
    if not isMinimized then return end
    
    if dragConnection then
        dragConnection:Disconnect()
        dragConnection = nil
    end
    
    if MinimizedGui and MinimizedGui:FindFirstChild("MinimizedFrame") then
        local tween = TweenService:Create(MinimizedGui.MinimizedFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)})
        tween:Play()
        tween.Completed:Wait()
        MinimizedGui:Destroy()
        MinimizedGui = nil
    end
    
    MainFrame.Visible = true
    isMinimized = false
end

local function minimizeGui()
    if isMinimized then return end
    isMinimized = true
    MainFrame.Visible = false
    
    MinimizedGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    MinimizedGui.Name = "MinimizedCheat"
    pcall(function() MinimizedGui.Parent = CoreGui end)
    if not MinimizedGui.Parent then MinimizedGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui") end

    -- Custom Drag Logic
    local dragging = false
    local dragStart = nil
    local startPos = nil
    local isClick = true
    
    RestoreBtn.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
            dragging = true
            isClick = true
            dragStart = input.Position
            startPos = MinimizedFrame.Position
            
            local inputConnection
            inputConnection = input.Changed:Connect(function()
                if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                    dragging = false
                    if inputConnection then inputConnection:Disconnect() end
                    if isClick then restoreGui() end
                end
            end)
        end
    end)
    
    dragConnection = UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
        if dragging then
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                local delta = input.Position - dragStart
                if delta.Magnitude > 5 then isClick = false end
                MinimizedFrame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    TweenService:Create(MinimizedFrame, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 80)}):Play()
end

-- Add Right Control key binding to minimize/restore
local function onInputBegan(input)
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.RightControl then
        if isMinimized then
            restoreGui()
        else
            minimizeGui()
        end
    end
end

    CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        Config.IsRunning = false
        for _, conn in pairs(Connections) do
            if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
        end
        table.clear(Connections)
        
        -- 1. Destroy UI
        if ScreenGui then ScreenGui:Destroy() end
        if ESPFolder then ESPFolder:Destroy() end
        if MinimizedGui then MinimizedGui:Destroy() end
        if BroadcastGui then BroadcastGui:Destroy() end
        if _G.SnowGui then _G.SnowGui:Destroy() end
        SendNotification("Cyberpunks has been destroyed", 3)
        
        -- 2. Disable Features
        for k, v in pairs(Config) do
            if type(v) == "boolean" then
                Config[k] = false
            end
        end
        
        -- 3. Cleanup Objects
        if FOVCircle then pcall(function() FOVCircle:Remove() end) end
        
        -- Destroy snow effect
        if SnowGui then SnowGui:Destroy() end
        if _G.SnowGui then _G.SnowGui:Destroy() end
        for _, c in pairs(SnowConnections) do if c then c:Disconnect() end end
        SnowConnections = {}
        
        -- 4. Reset Character
        if character and humanoid then
            if rootPart then
                rootPart.Anchored = false
                for _, v in pairs(rootPart:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:IsA("BodyVelocity") or v:IsA("BodyGyro") then v:Destroy() end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- 5. Disconnects
        if reachConnection then reachConnection:Disconnect() end
        if antiLavaConnection then antiLavaConnection:Disconnect() end
        if potatoConnection then potatoConnection:Disconnect() end
        pcall(function() RunService:UnbindFromRenderStep("AimLockPriority") end)
        pcall(function() script:Destroy() end)
        
        -- Attempt to stop external scripts
        pcall(function() _G.AutoFarm = false; _G.AutoFarmChest = false end)
    end)

    local function switchTab(tabName)
        for name, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do
            btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 30)
            btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
            btn.UIStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        end
        
        -- Clear Search when switching tabs
        if SearchBar.Text ~= "" then SearchBar.Text = "" end
        
        for name, page in pairs(Pages) do
            page.Visible = false
        end
        
        TabBtns[tabName].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        TabBtns[tabName].TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        TabBtns[tabName].UIStroke.Color = CurrentThemeColor
        Pages[tabName].Visible = true
    end

    -- Search Logic
    local allItems = {}
    local function InitSearch()
        allItems = {}
        for name, page in pairs(Pages) do
            if name ~= "Search" then
                local children = page:GetChildren()
                table.sort(children, function(a, b)
                    local orderA = (a:IsA("GuiObject") and a.LayoutOrder) or 0
                    local orderB = (b:IsA("GuiObject") and b.LayoutOrder) or 0
                    return orderA < orderB
                end)
                
                local currentSectionId = name .. "_0"
                local sectionCount = 0
                
                for _, child in ipairs(children) do
                    if not (child:IsA("UIListLayout") or child:IsA("UIPadding")) then
                    
                        -- Identify Section Header by Color (Specific to createSection: 80, 80, 90)
                        if child:IsA("TextLabel") and child.TextColor3 == Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 90) then
                            sectionCount = sectionCount + 1
                            currentSectionId = name .. "_" .. sectionCount
                        end
                        
                        table.insert(allItems, {
                            Obj = child,
                            OriginalParent = page,
                            SectionId = currentSectionId
                        })
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end

    SearchBar:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
        local text = SearchBar.Text:lower()
        if text == "" then
            if #allItems > 0 then
                for _, item in pairs(allItems) do
                    item.Obj.Parent = item.OriginalParent
                end
                allItems = {}
            end
            for name, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do
                if btn.BackgroundColor3 == Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45) then
                    Pages[name].Visible = true
                end
            end
            Pages.Search.Visible = false
        else
            if #allItems == 0 then InitSearch() end
            for _, page in pairs(Pages) do page.Visible = false end
            Pages.Search.Visible = true
            
            local matchingSections = {}
            for _, item in pairs(allItems) do
                local match = false
                if item.Obj:IsA("TextLabel") then
                    if item.Obj.Text:lower():find(text) then match = true end
                elseif item.Obj:IsA("Frame") then
                    for _, desc in pairs(item.Obj:GetDescendants()) do
                        if (desc:IsA("TextLabel") or desc:IsA("TextButton") or desc:IsA("TextBox")) and desc.Text:lower():find(text) then
                            match = true
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                if match then
                    matchingSections[item.SectionId] = true
                end
            end
            
            for _, item in pairs(allItems) do
                if matchingSections[item.SectionId] then
                    item.Obj.Parent = Pages.Search
                else
                    item.Obj.Parent = item.OriginalParent
                end
            end
        end
    end)
