    local isSocialsOpen = false
    local socialsLoop = nil
    local lastChatTime = 0 -- Pour dÃ©tecter les nouveaux messages
    local replyingTo = nil -- Variable pour stocker Ã  qui on rÃ©pond
    
    local function RefreshSocialsData(forceUI)
        local requestFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or (fluxus and fluxus.request) or request
        if requestFunc then
            local s, r = pcall(function() 
                return requestFunc({ 
                    Url = AUTH_URL .. "/socials/data?username=" .. HttpService:UrlEncode(player.Name) .. "&jobid=" .. tostring(game.JobId), 
                    Method = "GET" 
                }) 
            end)
            if s and r and r.StatusCode == 200 then
                local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(r.Body)
                if data then
                    OnlineLabel.Text = "Active Users: " .. (data.count or 0)
                    
                    if not isSocialsOpen and not forceUI then return end
                    
                    -- Update User List
                    for _, v in pairs(UserList:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("GuiObject") then v:Destroy() end end
                    if data.users then
                        for _, u in pairs(data.users) do
                            local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                            btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 15)
                            btn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                            btn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                            btn.TextSize = 9
                            btn.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                            btn.Text = "â€¢ " .. u
                            btn.Parent = UserList
                            
                            btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                                task.spawn(function()
                                    local s, r = pcall(function()
                                        return requestFunc({
                                            Url = AUTH_URL .. "/socials/chat",
                                            Method = "POST",
                                            Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                                            Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
                                                key = keyString, 
                                                name = player.Name, 
                                                message = "Pinged you",
                                                type = "ping",
                                                target = u
                                            })
                                        })
                                    end)
                                    if s and r and r.StatusCode == 200 then SendNotification("Ping sent!", 2) end
                                end)
                            end)
                        end
                    end

                    -- Update Chat
                    -- On vÃ©rifie si le dernier message a changÃ© ou si on force l'update
                    local currentMsgs = #ChatScroll:GetChildren() - 2 -- UIPadding & UIListLayout
                    local latestMsg = data.chat and data.chat[#data.chat]
                    local latestTime = latestMsg and latestMsg.time or 0
                    
                    if data.chat and (latestTime ~= lastChatTime or #data.chat ~= currentMsgs or forceUI) then
                        -- Notification Logic (Check for replies)
                        if lastChatTime > 0 then
                            for _, msg in pairs(data.chat) do
                                if msg.time > lastChatTime then
                                    if msg.replyTo and (msg.replyTo == player.Name or msg.replyTo == player.DisplayName) and msg.name ~= player.Name and msg.name ~= player.DisplayName then
                                        SendNotification(msg.name .. " answered you", 5)
                                    end
                                    
                                    if msg.type == "ping" and msg.target then
                                        local myEntry = (player.DisplayName or player.Name)
                                        if Config.IsWhitelisted then myEntry = "[WL] " .. myEntry end
                                        if msg.target == myEntry and msg.name ~= player.Name and msg.name ~= player.DisplayName then
                                            SendNotification(msg.name .. " pinged you", 5)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        lastChatTime = latestTime
                        for _, v in pairs(ChatScroll:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("Frame") then v:Destroy() end end
                        for _, msg in pairs(data.chat) do
                            if not msg.type or msg.type == "chat" then
                            local msgFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                            msgFrame.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
                            msgFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 0)
                            msgFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            msgFrame.Parent = ChatScroll
                            
                            -- Click to Reply (Invisible Button covering the message)
                            local replyBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                            replyBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                            replyBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            replyBtn.Text = ""
                            replyBtn.Parent = msgFrame
                            replyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                                replyingTo = msg.name
                                ChatInput.PlaceholderText = "Replying to " .. msg.name .. "..."
                                ChatInput:CaptureFocus()
                            end)
                            
                            local nameLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                            nameLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 12)
                            nameLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            nameLbl.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                            nameLbl.TextSize = 9
                            nameLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                            local timeStr = msg.time and os.date("[%H:%M] ", math.floor(msg.time / 1000)) or ""
                            local roleText = ""
                            if msg.role == "WL" or msg.role == "WL-AD" then roleText = " [WL]" end
                            if msg.role == "AD" or msg.role == "WL-AD" then roleText = roleText .. " [AD]" end
                            nameLbl.Text = timeStr .. msg.name .. roleText .. ":"
                            nameLbl.TextColor3 = (msg.role == "WL" or msg.role == "WL-AD") and Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) or (msg.role == "AD" and Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 0) or CurrentThemeColor)
                            nameLbl.Parent = msgFrame
                            
                            local contentLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                            contentLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0)
                            contentLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 12)
                            contentLbl.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
                            contentLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            contentLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                            contentLbl.TextSize = 9
                            contentLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                            contentLbl.TextWrapped = true
                            contentLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(230, 230, 230)
                            contentLbl.Text = msg.msg
                            contentLbl.Parent = msgFrame
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait() -- Attendre le rendu
                        ChatScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, 9e9) -- Force le scroll tout en bas
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Background Social Loop (Always active to keep count updated)
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            RefreshSocialsData(isSocialsOpen)
            task.wait(1) -- Auto-refresh every 1 second
        end
    end)
    
    SocialsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()

        RightTabContainer.Visible = false

    end)
    
    SendBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local msg = ChatInput.Text
        if msg == "" then return end
        ChatInput.Text = ""
        
        local currentReply = replyingTo
        replyingTo = nil
        ChatInput.PlaceholderText = "Message..."

        local requestFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or (fluxus and fluxus.request) or request
        if requestFunc and keyString then
            task.spawn(function()
                local s, r = pcall(function()
                    return requestFunc({
                        Url = AUTH_URL .. "/socials/chat",
                        Method = "POST",
                        Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                         Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
                            key = keyString, 
                            name = player.Name, 
                            message = msg,
                            role = (Config.IsWhitelisted and "WL" or "") .. (Config.IsAdmin and "AD" or ""),
                            replyTo = currentReply
                        })
                    })
                end)
                if s and r and r.StatusCode == 200 then 
                    SendNotification("Message Sent!", 1) 
                else
                    SendNotification("Failed to send message", 2)
                end
                task.wait(0.2)
                RefreshSocialsData(true)
            end)
        end
    end)

    if keyDuration and keyDuration < 800000000 then
        task.spawn(function()
            local endTime = tick() + keyDuration
            while Config.IsRunning and tick() < endTime do
                local rem = endTime - tick()
                local h = math.floor(rem / 3600)
                local m = math.floor((rem % 3600) / 60)
                local s = math.floor(rem % 60)
                KeyTimeLabel.Text = string.format("Expires: %02d:%02d:%02d", h, m, s)
                task.wait(1)
            end
            if tick() >= endTime then player:Kick("Key Expired") end
        end)
    end

    -- Helper to manage Left Panel Tabs
    local function setLeftTabs(mode)
        for _, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do btn.Visible = false end
        
        if mode == "PVP" then
            TabBtns.Players.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Visuals.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Aim.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Hitbox.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Teleport.Visible = true
            for _, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do btn.Size = UDim2.new(0.2, -4, 1, 0) end
            switchTab("Players")
        elseif mode == "Farm" then
            TabBtns.FarmScripts.Visible = true
            TabBtns.FarmSettings.Visible = true
            TabBtns.FarmStatus.Visible = true
            TabBtns.FarmFarming.Visible = true
            for _, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do 
                if btn.Visible then btn.Size = UDim2.new(0.25, -4, 1, 0) end 
            end
            switchTab("FarmScripts")
        elseif mode == "Dungeon" then
            TabBtns.Raid.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Raid.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            switchTab("Raid")
        elseif mode == "Settings" then
            TabBtns.Settings.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Settings.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            switchTab("Settings")
        elseif mode == "Shop" then
            TabBtns.Shop.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Shop.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            switchTab("Shop")
        elseif mode == "SeaEvent" then
            TabBtns.SeaEvent.Visible = true
            TabBtns.SeaEvent.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            switchTab("SeaEvent")
        elseif mode == "Custom" then
            TabBtns.Custom.Visible = true
            TabBtns.Custom.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            switchTab("Custom")
        end
    end

    end)
    
    PVPBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setLeftTabs("PVP")
    end)
    
    ShopBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setLeftTabs("Shop")
    end)
    
    CustomBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setLeftTabs("Custom")
    end)

    SettingsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        setLeftTabs("Settings")
    end)
    
    switchTab("Players")

    -- === UI ELEMENTS CREATION ===

    local function createSection(parent, text, order)
        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text:upper()
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 90)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Label.TextSize = 8
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.LayoutOrder = order
        Label.Parent = parent
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 2)
        Pad.Parent = Label
    end

    local function createKeybind(parent, text, configKey, order)
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        Frame.LayoutOrder = order
        Frame.Parent = parent

        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        Corner.Parent = Frame
        
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        Stroke.Thickness = 1
        Stroke.Parent = Frame

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(0.7, 0, 1, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.TextSize = (text == "One Shot (Need Anti Haunted)") and 7 or 9
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
        Pad.Parent = Label

        local Button = Instance.new("TextButton")
        Button.Size = UDim2.new(0.25, 0, 0.7, 0)
        Button.Position = UDim2.new(0.72, 0, 0.15, 0)
        Button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
        Button.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        Button.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Button.TextSize = 8
        Button.Parent = Frame
        Button.ZIndex = 100
        
        local key = Config[configKey]
        local keyName = "..."
        if key and typeof(key) == "EnumItem" then
            if key ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
                keyName = key.Name
            end
        end
        Button.Text = keyName
        KeybindButtons[configKey] = Button
        
        local BCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        BCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        BCorner.Parent = Button
        
        local BStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        BStroke.Color = CurrentThemeColor
        BStroke.Thickness = 1.5
        BStroke.Transparency = 0.7
        BStroke.Parent = Button

        local isWaitingForKey = false

        Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if isWaitingForKey then return end
            
            isWaitingForKey = true
            Button.Text = "Press a key..."
            Button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 80)
            BStroke.Transparency = 0.3
            
            local oldKeyCode = Config[configKey]
            local connection
            connection = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
                if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
                    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Escape then
                        -- Annuler - revenir Ã  l'ancienne touche
                        Config[configKey] = oldKeyCode
                        if oldKeyCode and typeof(oldKeyCode) == "EnumItem" and oldKeyCode ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
                            Button.Text = oldKeyCode.Name
                        else
                            Button.Text = "..."
                        end
                        Button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
                        BStroke.Transparency = 0.7
                        isWaitingForKey = false
                        connection:Disconnect()
                    else
                        -- Assigner la nouvelle touche
                        Config[configKey] = input.KeyCode
                        Button.Text = input.KeyCode.Name
                        Button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
                        BStroke.Transparency = 0.7
                        isWaitingForKey = false
                        connection:Disconnect()
                    end
                end
            end)
        end)
    end

    local function createInput(parent, text, configKey, order)
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        Frame.LayoutOrder = order
        Frame.Parent = parent

        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        Corner.Parent = Frame
        
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        Stroke.Thickness = 1
        Stroke.Parent = Frame

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.TextSize = 9
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
        Pad.Parent = Label

        local Input = Instance.new("TextBox")
        Input.Size = UDim2.new(0.35, 0, 0.7, 0)
        Input.Position = UDim2.new(0.62, 0, 0.15, 0)
        Input.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
        Input.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        Input.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Input.TextSize = 8
        Input.Text = tostring(Config[configKey])
        Input.Parent = Frame

        InputBoxes[configKey] = Input

        local ICorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        ICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        ICorner.Parent = Input

        Input.FocusLost:Connect(function()
            if type(Config[configKey]) == "string" then
                Config[configKey] = Input.Text:gsub("^%s*(.-)%s*$", "%1") -- Trim spaces
                if configKey == "CustomCursorId" then
                    local val = Config[configKey]
                    if val ~= "" then
                        if tonumber(val) then
                            mouse.Icon = "rbxassetid://" .. val
                        else
                            mouse.Icon = val
                        end
                    else
                        mouse.Icon = ""
                    end
                end
                
                if configKey == "AutoLoadConfigName" then
                    UpdateLoaderSettings()
                end
            else
                local num = tonumber(Input.Text)
                if num then
                    -- LIMITES DE VITESSE
                    if configKey == "FlySpeedValue" and num > 1000 then num = 1000 end
                    if configKey == "DesyncFlySpeed" and num > 355 then num = 355 end
                    
                    Config[configKey] = num
                    if configKey == "FOVValue" and num > 120 then num = 120 end
                    if configKey == "FOVValue" and num < 10 then num = 10 end
                    
                    if configKey == "JumpPowerValue" then
                        if humanoid then humanoid.UseJumpPower = true humanoid.JumpPower = num end
                    end
                    
                    Input.Text = tostring(num)
                    
                    if (configKey == "TorsoSize" or configKey == "TorsoTransparency") and Config.HitboxPreset then
                        local s = Config.TorsoSize
                        local t = Config.TorsoTransparency
                        local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if root then 
                            root.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                            root.Transparency = t
                            root.CanTouch = true -- Must be true for TP Hit to work on touch
                            root.CanQuery = false
                        end
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") and (v.Name == "Torso" or v.Name == "UpperTorso" or v.Name == "LowerTorso") then
                                v.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                                v.Transparency = t
                                v.CanTouch = true
                                v.CanQuery = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    
                    if configKey == "DungeonRange" and Config.KillDungeon then
                        local s = Config.DungeonRange
                        local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if root then root.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s) end
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") and (v.Name:find("Arm") or v.Name:find("Hand")) then
                                v.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                else
                    Input.Text = tostring(Config[configKey])
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    
    local function createToggle(parent, text, configKey, order)
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        Frame.LayoutOrder = order
        Frame.Parent = parent

        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        Corner.Parent = Frame
        
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        Stroke.Thickness = 1
        Stroke.Parent = Frame

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(0.8, 0, 1, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.TextSize = 9
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
        Pad.Parent = Label

        local Button = Instance.new("TextButton")
        Button.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20)
        Button.Position = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0.5, -10)
        Button.BackgroundColor3 = Config[configKey] and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        Button.Text = ""
        Button.Parent = Frame
        
        local BCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        BCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
        BCorner.Parent = Button
        
        -- Store button for external updates
        ToggleButtons[configKey] = Button

        Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            Config[configKey] = not Config[configKey]
            Button.BackgroundColor3 = Config[configKey] and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            
            if configKey == "ToolColorChanger" and not Config.ToolColorChanger then
                if character then
                    restoreToolColor(character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool"))
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "PotatoGraphics" then
                local isLow = Config.PotatoGraphics
                
                -- Fast Flags / Quality
                if isLow then
                    renderSettings.QualityLevel = Enum.QualityLevel.Level01
                    renderSettings.MeshPartDetailLevel = Enum.MeshPartDetailLevel.Level01
                else
                    renderSettings.QualityLevel = Enum.QualityLevel.Automatic
                    renderSettings.MeshPartDetailLevel = Enum.MeshPartDetailLevel.Level04
                end
                
                pcall(function()
                    Lighting.GlobalShadows = not isLow
                    Lighting.Outlines = not isLow
                    Terrain.Decoration = not isLow
                    
                    potatoDOF.Enabled = isLow
                    potatoColor.Enabled = isLow
                    
                    Terrain.WaterWaveSize = isLow and 0 or 0.15
                    Terrain.WaterWaveSpeed = isLow and 0 or 10
                    Terrain.WaterReflectance = isLow and 0 or 1
                    Terrain.WaterTransparency = isLow and 0 or 1
                end)
                
                -- Iterate Workspace
                task.spawn(function()
                    for _, obj in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        makePotato(obj)
                    end
                end)
                
                -- Connection
                if isLow then
                    if not potatoConnection then
                        potatoConnection = workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(obj)
                            task.defer(function() makePotato(obj) end)
                        end)
                    end
                else
                    if potatoConnection then
                        potatoConnection:Disconnect()
                        potatoConnection = nil
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "HitboxPreset" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local hum = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                    local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    local ProximityPromptService = game:GetService("ProximityPromptService")
                    
                    if Config.HitboxPreset then
                        -- Disable Sitting
                        if hum then hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false) end
                        
                        -- Disable Interactions (Proximity & Touch)
                        ProximityPromptService.Enabled = false
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanTouch = false end
                        end
                        
                        -- Big Torso Mode (Skin Glitch)
                        local s = Config.TorsoSize
                        local t = Config.TorsoTransparency
                        if root then
                            root.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                            root.Transparency = t
                            root.CanCollide = false
                            root.CanTouch = true -- Enable touch for TP Hit logic
                            root.CanQuery = false -- Prevent mouse blocking
                        end
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") and (v.Name == "Torso" or v.Name == "UpperTorso" or v.Name == "LowerTorso") then
                                v.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                                v.Transparency = t
                                v.CanCollide = false
                                v.CanTouch = true
                                v.CanQuery = false
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        -- Reset
                        if hum then hum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true) end
                        ProximityPromptService.Enabled = true
                        
                        local success, desc = pcall(function()
                            return Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(player.UserId)
                        end)
                        if success and desc and hum then
                            ApplyDescriptionCustom(hum, desc)
                            if root then
                                root.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
                                root.Transparency = 1
                                root.CanCollide = true
                                root.CanTouch = true
                                root.CanQuery = true
                            end
                            -- Reset All Parts
                            for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    v.CanTouch = true
                                    v.CanQuery = true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
            
            -- Infinite FlashStep: Set FlashstepCooldown attribute
            if configKey == "InfiniteFlashStep" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    if Config.InfiniteFlashStep then
                        -- Set cooldown to 10 when enabled
                        char:SetAttribute("FlashstepCooldown", 10)
                    else
                        -- Reset to 0 when disabled
                        char:SetAttribute("FlashstepCooldown", 0)
                    end
                end)
            end
            
            -- Infinite Zoom: Set CameraMaxZoomDistance
            if configKey == "InfiniteZoom" then
                if Config.InfiniteZoom then
                    player.CameraMaxZoomDistance = 100000
                    player.CameraMinZoomDistance = 0.5
                else
                    player.CameraMaxZoomDistance = 100
                    player.CameraMinZoomDistance = 0.5
                end
            end
            
            -- Ice Water: Set WaterWalking attribute
            if configKey == "IceWater" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    if Config.IceWater then
                        char:SetAttribute("WaterWalking", true)
                    else
                        char:SetAttribute("WaterWalking", false)
                    end
                end)
            end
            
            -- Unbreakable All: Set UnbreakableAll attribute
            if configKey == "UnbreakableAll" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    if Config.UnbreakableAll then
                        char:SetAttribute("UnbreakableAll", true)
                    else
                        char:SetAttribute("UnbreakableAll", false)
                    end
                end)
            end
            
            if configKey == "KillDungeon" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    
                    if Config.KillDungeon then
                        local s = Config.DungeonRange
                        if root then
                            root.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                            root.Transparency = 0.5
                            root.CanCollide = false
                        end
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") and (v.Name:find("Arm") or v.Name:find("Hand")) then
                                v.Size = Vector3.new(s, s, s)
                                v.Transparency = 0.5
                                v.CanCollide = false
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        if root then
                            root.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
                            root.Transparency = 1
                            root.CanCollide = true
                        end
                        local success, desc = pcall(function() return Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(player.UserId) end)
                        if success and desc and humanoid then ApplyDescriptionCustom(humanoid, desc) end
                    end
                end)
            end
            
            if configKey == "FarmNearest" then
                if Config.FarmNearest then
                    Config.Reach = true
                    Config.ReachSize = 10
                    Config.ReachTransparency = 1
                    if ToggleButtons["Reach"] then ToggleButtons["Reach"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor end
                    if InputBoxes["ReachSize"] then InputBoxes["ReachSize"].Text = tostring(Config.ReachSize) end
                else
                    Config.Reach = false
                    Config.ReachSize = 1
                    if ToggleButtons["Reach"] then ToggleButtons["Reach"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) end
                    if InputBoxes["ReachSize"] then InputBoxes["ReachSize"].Text = "1" end
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "TeleportTool" then
                if Config.TeleportTool then
                    local tool = Instance.new("Tool")
                    tool.Name = "EPOteleporter"
                    tool.RequiresHandle = false
                    tool.ToolTip = "Click to Teleport"
                    
                    tool.Activated:Connect(function()
                        if player.Character then
                            local hrp = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local m = player:GetMouse()
                            if hrp and m then
                                local targetPos = m.Hit.p
                                local originalLook = hrp.CFrame.LookVector
                                player.Character:PivotTo(CFrame.new(targetPos))
                                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos, targetPos + originalLook)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    tool.Parent = player.Backpack
                else
                    if player.Backpack:FindFirstChild("EPOteleporter") then player.Backpack.EPOteleporter:Destroy() end
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("EPOteleporter") then player.Character.EPOteleporter:Destroy() end
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "DashLengthEnabled" and not Config.DashLengthEnabled then
                if character then
                    character:SetAttribute("DashLength", 1)
                    character:SetAttribute("DashLengthAir", 1)
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "DisableSnow" then
                if _G.SnowGui then
                    _G.SnowGui.Enabled = not Config.DisableSnow
                end
                UpdateLoaderSettings()
            end
            
            if configKey == "AutoLoadConfig" then
                UpdateLoaderSettings()
            end
            
            -- Instant Respawn toggle binding
            if configKey == "InstantRespawn" then
                if Config.InstantRespawn then
                    BindInstantRespawn()
                else
                    if instantRespawnConn then instantRespawnConn:Disconnect(); instantRespawnConn = nil end
                end
            end
            
            if configKey == "HandleExtender" and not Config.HandleExtender then
                local function restoreHandle(tool)
                    if tool and tool:IsA("Tool") then
                        for _, part in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                                part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize")
                                part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", nil)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if player.Character then
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Character:GetChildren()) do restoreHandle(t) end
                    local armParts = {"Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg", "LeftHand", "RightHand", "LeftLowerArm", "LeftUpperArm", "RightLowerArm", "RightUpperArm", "LeftLowerLeg", "LeftUpperLeg", "LeftFoot", "RightLowerLeg", "RightUpperLeg", "RightFoot"}
                    for _, name in pairs(armParts) do
                        local part = player.Character:FindFirstChild(name)
                        if part and part:IsA("BasePart") and part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                            part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize")
                            part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", nil)
                        end
                    end
                end
                if player.Backpack then
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Backpack:GetChildren()) do restoreHandle(t) end
                end
            end
        end)
    end
    
    local function createCycle(parent, text, configKey, options, order)
        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        Frame.LayoutOrder = order
        Frame.Parent = parent

        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        Corner.Parent = Frame
        
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        Stroke.Thickness = 1
        Stroke.Parent = Frame

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(0.6, 0, 1, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.TextSize = 9
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
        Pad.Parent = Label

        local Button = Instance.new("TextButton")
        Button.Size = UDim2.new(0.35, 0, 0.7, 0)
        Button.Position = UDim2.new(0.62, 0, 0.15, 0)
        Button.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
        Button.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        Button.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        Button.TextSize = 8
        Button.Text = Config[configKey]
        Button.Parent = Frame

        local BCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        BCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        BCorner.Parent = Button

        Button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local currentIndex = 1
            for i, v in ipairs(options) do
                if v == Config[configKey] then currentIndex = i break end
            end
            currentIndex = currentIndex + 1
            if currentIndex > #options then currentIndex = 1 end
            Config[configKey] = options[currentIndex]
            Button.Text = Config[configKey]
        end)
        return Button
    end

    local function restoreToolColor(tool)
        if not tool or not tool:IsA("Tool") then return end
        for _, descendant in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
            if descendant:IsA("BasePart") then
                local originalColor = descendant:GetAttribute("OriginalColor")
                if originalColor then
                    descendant.Color = originalColor
                    descendant:SetAttribute("OriginalColor", nil)
                end
            elseif descendant:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or descendant:IsA("Trail") or descendant:IsA("Beam") then
                local originalCS = descendant:GetAttribute("OriginalColorSequence")
                if originalCS then
                    descendant.Color = originalCS
                    descendant:SetAttribute("OriginalColorSequence", nil)
                end
            elseif descendant:IsA("Light") then
                local originalLightColor = descendant:GetAttribute("OriginalLightColor")
                if originalLightColor then
                    descendant.Color = originalLightColor
                    descendant:SetAttribute("OriginalLightColor", nil)
                end
            end
        end
    end

    local function createSlider(parent, text, configKey, order, min, max, default)
        Config[configKey] = Config[configKey] or default

        local Frame = Instance.new("Frame")
        Frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 40)
        Frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        Frame.LayoutOrder = order
        Frame.Parent = parent

        local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        Corner.Parent = Frame
        
        local Stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
        Stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(35, 35, 45)
        Stroke.Thickness = 1
        Stroke.Parent = Frame

        local Label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        Label.Text = text
        Label.Size = UDim2.new(0.7, 0, 0, 20)
        Label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        Label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.TextSize = 9
        Label.Parent = Frame
        
        local Pad = Instance.new("UIPadding")
        Pad.PaddingLeft = UDim.new(0, 10)
        Pad.Parent = Label

        local ValueLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
        ValueLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0.3, -10, 0, 20)
        ValueLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.7, 0, 0, 0)
        ValueLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        ValueLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        ValueLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        ValueLabel.TextSize = 8
        ValueLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right
        ValueLabel.Parent = Frame

        local SliderBack = Instance.new("Frame")
        SliderBack.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 4)
        SliderBack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 25)
        SliderBack.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        SliderBack.Parent = Frame
        local SBCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") SBCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0) SBCorner.Parent = SliderBack

        local SliderFront = Instance.new("Frame")
        SliderFront.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0)
        SliderFront.BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        SliderFront.Parent = SliderBack
        local SFCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") SFCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0) SFCorner.Parent = SliderFront

        local Thumb = Instance.new("TextButton")
        Thumb.Size = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0, 12)
        Thumb.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        Thumb.Text = ""
        Thumb.ZIndex = 2
        Thumb.Parent = SliderBack -- Parent to SliderBack, not SliderFront
        local TCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") TCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0) TCorner.Parent = Thumb

        local function updateSliderFromValue(value)
            local percentage = (value - min) / (max - min)
            percentage = math.clamp(percentage, 0, 1)
            SliderFront.Size = UDim2.new(percentage, 0, 1, 0)
            -- Position thumb at the right edge of SliderFront
            Thumb.Position = UDim2.new(0, math.floor(SliderBack.AbsoluteSize.X * percentage - 6), 0.5, -6)
            ValueLabel.Text = string.format("%.2f", value)
            Config[configKey] = value
        end

        local function updateSliderFromPosition(input)
            local mousePos = input.Position
            local relativePos = mousePos.X - SliderBack.AbsolutePosition.X
            local percentage = math.clamp(relativePos / SliderBack.AbsoluteSize.X, 0, 1)
            local newValue = min + (max - min) * percentage
            updateSliderFromValue(newValue)
        end

        updateSliderFromValue(Config[configKey])

        Thumb.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
            if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                local dragConn, releaseConn
                dragConn = UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(changedInput)
                    if changedInput.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or changedInput.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                        updateSliderFromPosition(changedInput)
                    end
                end)
                releaseConn = UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(endedInput)
                    if endedInput.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or endedInput.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
                        dragConn:Disconnect()
                        releaseConn:Disconnect()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
        
        return Frame
    end

    local function createInfo(parent, text, order)

        Label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
        Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1

        Label.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        Label.TextSize = 8
        Label.LayoutOrder = order
        Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
        Label.Parent = parent
    end

    do

        local VizFrame = nil
        
        VizBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if not VizFrame then
                -- Create Window
                VizFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
                VizFrame.Name = "PlayerVisualizer"
                VizFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 350, 0, 400)
                VizFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -175, 0.5, -200)
                VizFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 15, 20)
                VizFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                VizFrame.Active = true
                VizFrame.Draggable = true
                VizFrame.Visible = true
                VizFrame.Parent = ScreenGui
                
                local Corner = Instance.new("UICorner") Corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6) Corner.Parent = VizFrame

                Header.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
                Header.Parent = VizFrame

                CloseBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                CloseBtn.TextSize = 12
                CloseBtn.Parent = Header
                CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() VizFrame.Visible = false end)
                
                -- Search
                local SearchBox = Instance.new("TextBox")
                SearchBox.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 25)
                SearchBox.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 35)
                SearchBox.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
                SearchBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                SearchBox.PlaceholderText = "Search Player..."
                SearchBox.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                SearchBox.TextSize = 10
                SearchBox.Parent = VizFrame
                Instance.new("UICorner", SearchBox).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                
                -- List
                local List = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
                List.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 1, -70)
                List.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 65)
                List.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                List.BorderSizePixel = 0
                List.ScrollBarThickness = 4
                List.Parent = VizFrame
                
                local ListLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
                ListLayout.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder
                ListLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 5)
                ListLayout.Parent = List
                
                local function colorText(text, color)
                    local r, g, b = math.floor(color.R*255), math.floor(color.G*255), math.floor(color.B*255)
                    return string.format('<font color="rgb(%d,%d,%d)">%s</font>', r, g, b, text)
                end
                
                local function UpdateList()
                    if not VizFrame.Visible then return end
                    
                    for _, v in pairs(List:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("Frame") then v:Destroy() end end
                    
                    local filter = SearchBox.Text:lower()
                    
                    for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if filter == "" or p.Name:lower():find(filter) or p.DisplayName:lower():find(filter) then
                            local char = p.Character
                            
                            local Entry = Instance.new("Frame")
                            Entry.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 70)
                            Entry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 30)
                            Entry.Parent = List
                            Instance.new("UICorner", Entry).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4)
                            
                            local Avatar = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
                            Avatar.Size = UDim2.new(0, 50, 0, 50)
                            Avatar.Position = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 10)
                            Avatar.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            Avatar.Image = "rbxthumb://type=AvatarHeadShot&id=" .. p.UserId .. "&w=150&h=150"
                            Avatar.Parent = Entry
                            Instance.new("UICorner", Avatar).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
                            
                            local InfoLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
                            InfoLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -65, 1, -5)
                            InfoLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 2)
                            InfoLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            InfoLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                            InfoLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                            InfoLabel.TextSize = 8
                            InfoLabel.RichText = true
                            InfoLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
                            InfoLabel.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top
                            InfoLabel.Parent = Entry
                            
                            local hpText = colorText("N/A", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            local v4Text = colorText("Inactive", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            local pvpText = colorText("Unk", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            local dodgeText = colorText("0", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            local fruitText = colorText("None", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            local islandText = colorText("Unk", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                            
                            if char then
                                local hum = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if hum then
                                    local hp = math.floor(hum.Health)
                                    local maxHp = math.floor(hum.MaxHealth)
                                    local hpColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100)
                                    if hp < maxHp * 0.3 then hpColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                                    elseif hp < maxHp * 0.7 then hpColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 0) end
                                    hpText = colorText(hp .. "/" .. maxHp, hpColor)
                                end
                                
                                local v4Obj = char:FindFirstChild("RaceTransformed")
                                if v4Obj and v4Obj:IsA("BoolValue") and v4Obj.Value then 
                                    v4Text = colorText("Active", Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0))
                                else
                                    v4Text = colorText("Inactive", Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0))
                                end
                                
                                -- Fruit Detection (Equipped or Backpack)
                                local foundFruit = false
                                local fName = "None"
                                for _, t in pairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                                    if t:IsA("Tool") and t.ToolTip == "Blox Fruit" then
                                        fName = t.Name
                                        foundFruit = true
                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                                if not foundFruit then
                                    local bp = p:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                                    if bp then
                                        for _, t in pairs(bp:GetChildren()) do
                                            if t:IsA("Tool") and t.ToolTip == "Blox Fruit" then
                                                fName = t.Name
                                                break
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                                if fName ~= "None" then
                                    fruitText = colorText(fName, Color3.fromRGB(200, 100, 255))
                                end
                                
                                -- PVP / Safe Zone / InCombat
                                local inCombat = false
                                local inCombatText = "No"
                                
                                -- Check InCombat attribute on character (character -> attributes -> InCombat)
                                local inCombatAttr = char:GetAttribute("InCombat")
                                if inCombatAttr ~= nil then
                                    inCombat = inCombatAttr
                                    inCombatText = inCombatAttr and "Yes" or "No"
                                end
                                
                                if char:FindFirstChildOfClass("ForceField") then
                                    pvpText = colorText("Safe Zone", Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 255))
                                else
                                    local pvpAttr = char:GetAttribute("PvP")
                                    if pvpAttr == nil then
                                        local pvpVal = char:FindFirstChild("PvP")
                                        if pvpVal and pvpVal:IsA("BoolValue") then pvpAttr = pvpVal.Value end
                                    end
                                    
                                    if pvpAttr ~= nil then
                                        if pvpAttr then
                                            pvpText = colorText("On", Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50))
                                        else
                                            pvpText = colorText("Off", Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100))
                                        end
                                    else
                                        -- Try checking Data folder if available (some games)
                                        local d = p:FindFirstChild("Data")
                                        local dPvp = d and d:FindFirstChild("PvP")
                                        if dPvp then
                                            if dPvp.Value then pvpText = colorText("On", Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50))
                                            else pvpText = colorText("Off", Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100)) end
                                        else
                                            pvpText = colorText("Unk", Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150))
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Replace "Unk" after PVP with just Yes/No for InCombat
                                local combatColor = inCombat and Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50) or Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 100)
                                pvpText = colorText(inCombatText, combatColor)
                                
                                -- Dodge (Observation) - Now checks KenDodgesLeft and KenMaxDodges attributes first
                                local dVal = 0
                                local maxDVal = 0
                                
                                -- First, check for Ken attributes on player (player -> attributes -> KenDodgesLeft/KenMaxDodges)
                                local kenDodgesLeft = p:GetAttribute("KenDodgesLeft")
                                local kenMaxDodges = p:GetAttribute("KenMaxDodges")
                                
                                if kenDodgesLeft ~= nil and kenMaxDodges ~= nil then
                                    -- Use Ken attributes (priority)
                                    dVal = kenDodgesLeft
                                    maxDVal = kenMaxDodges
                                else
                                    -- Fallback to old observation system
                                    local vision = p:FindFirstChild("VisionRadius")
                                    if vision and vision:IsA("ValueBase") then
                                        local exp = vision.Value
                                        if exp < 50 then maxDVal = 2
                                        elseif exp < 330 then maxDVal = 3
                                        elseif exp < 815 then maxDVal = 4
                                        elseif exp < 1417 then maxDVal = 5
                                        elseif exp < 2121 then maxDVal = 6
                                        elseif exp < 2824 then maxDVal = 7
                                        else maxDVal = 8 end
                                    end
                                    
                                    local obs = char:FindFirstChild("Observation") or char:FindFirstChild("ObservationV2")
                                    if not obs then
                                        for _, c in pairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                                            local n = string.lower(c.Name)
                                            if c:IsA("ValueBase") and (string.find(n, "observation") or string.find(n, "instinct")) then
                                                obs = c
                                                break
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                    
                                    if obs and obs:IsA("ValueBase") then 
                                        dVal = obs.Value 
                                    elseif maxDVal > 0 then
                                        dVal = maxDVal
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                if maxDVal > 0 then
                                    dodgeText = colorText(dVal .. "/" .. maxDVal, Color3.fromRGB(100, 200, 255))
                                else
                                    if dVal == 0 then
                                        local d = p:FindFirstChild("Data")
                                        local dObs = d and d:FindFirstChild("Observation")
                                        if dObs and dObs:IsA("ValueBase") then dVal = dObs.Value end
                                    end
                                    dodgeText = colorText(tostring(dVal), Color3.fromRGB(100, 200, 255))
                                end
                                
                                -- Island Player (CurrentLocation)
                                local locationAttr = p:GetAttribute("CurrentLocation")
                                if locationAttr ~= nil and locationAttr ~= "" then
                                    islandText = colorText(tostring(locationAttr), Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100))
                                end
                            end
                            
                            InfoLabel.Text = "<b>" .. p.DisplayName .. "</b> (@" .. p.Name .. ")\n" ..
                                             "ðŸ’š HP: " .. hpText .. " | âš¡ V4: " .. v4Text .. "\n" ..
                                             "âš”ï¸ PVP: " .. pvpText .. " | ðŸ‘ï¸ Dodge: " .. dodgeText .. "\n" ..
                                             "ðŸŽ Fruit: " .. fruitText .. " | ðŸï¸ Island: " .. islandText
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                SearchBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(UpdateList)
                
                task.spawn(function()
                    while Config.IsRunning and VizFrame do
                        if VizFrame.Visible then UpdateList() end
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    end
                end)
                
                UpdateList()
            else
                VizFrame.Visible = not VizFrame.Visible
            end
        end)
    end

        if shadersEnabled then
            -- Apply Effects
            for _, effect in pairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
                if effect:IsA("PostEffect") or effect:IsA("BloomEffect") then
                    effect:Destroy()
                end
            end

            local bloom = Instance.new("BloomEffect", Lighting)
            bloom.Intensity = 1
            bloom.Threshold = 0.5
            bloom.Size = 24
            bloom.Name = "Cyber_Bloom"

            local depthOfField = Instance.new("DepthOfFieldEffect", Lighting)
            depthOfField.FarIntensity = 0.25
            depthOfField.FocusDistance = 20
            depthOfField.InFocusRadius = 50
            depthOfField.NearIntensity = 0.75
            depthOfField.Name = "Cyber_DOF"

            local colorCorrection = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect", Lighting)
            colorCorrection.Brightness = 0.05
            colorCorrection.Contrast = 0.3
            colorCorrection.Saturation = 1.2
            colorCorrection.Name = "Cyber_CC"

            local sunRays = Instance.new("SunRaysEffect", Lighting)
            sunRays.Intensity = 0.12
            sunRays.Spread = 0.05
            sunRays.Name = "Cyber_Sun"

            Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(128, 128, 128)
            Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
            Lighting.Brightness = 1.8
            Lighting.ClockTime = 14
            
            if not reflectanceApplied then
                reflectanceApplied = true
                for _, part in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and not part:IsA("Terrain") and part.Reflectance < 0.1 then
                        part.Reflectance = 0.05
                    end
                end
            end
        else
            -- Remove Effects
            for _, effect in pairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
                if effect.Name:find("Cyber_") then
                    effect:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    end

        local RC_C = Instance.new("UICorner") RC_C.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) RC_C.Parent = ResetCharBtn
        
        -- Logic from provided script
        local function clearVisuals(char)
            for _, inst in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                if inst:IsA("Accessory") or inst:IsA("Hat") or inst:IsA("Shirt") or inst:IsA("Pants") or inst:IsA("ShirtGraphic") or inst:IsA("CharacterMesh") then
                    inst:Destroy()
                end
            end
            local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if head then
                for _, d in ipairs(head:GetChildren()) do
                    if d:IsA("Decal") and d.Name:lower() == "face" then d:Destroy() end
                end
            end
            local bc = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyColors")
            if bc then bc:Destroy() end
        end

        local function attachAccessory(char, accessory)
            local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
            if not handle then return end
            local targetAttachment, accAttachment
            for _, part in ipairs(char:GetChildren()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                    for _, att in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do
                        if att:IsA("Attachment") then
                            local match = handle:FindFirstChild(att.Name)
                            if match and match:IsA("Attachment") then
                                targetAttachment = att; accAttachment = match; break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if targetAttachment then break end
            end
            if targetAttachment and accAttachment then
                handle.CFrame = targetAttachment.WorldCFrame * accAttachment.CFrame:Inverse()
            else
                local root = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if root then handle.CFrame = root.CFrame end
            end
            local weld = Instance.new("WeldConstraint")
            weld.Part0 = handle
            weld.Part1 = (targetAttachment and targetAttachment.Parent) or char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or char:FindFirstChild("Head")
            weld.Parent = handle
            accessory.Parent = char
        end

        ApplySkinBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local uid = tonumber(Config.SkinChangerID)
            if not uid then SendNotification("Invalid User ID", 2) return end
            local char = player.Character
            if not char then return end
            
            local ok, model = pcall(function() return Players:GetCharacterAppearanceAsync(uid) end)
            if not ok or not model then SendNotification("Failed to fetch skin", 2) return end
            
            clearVisuals(char)
            local bc = model:FindFirstChildOfClass("BodyColors")
            if bc then bc:Clone().Parent = char end
            for _, item in ipairs(model:GetChildren()) do
                if item:IsA("Shirt") or item:IsA("Pants") or item:IsA("ShirtGraphic") then item:Clone().Parent = char end
            end
            for _, acc in ipairs(model:GetChildren()) do
                if acc:IsA("Accessory") or acc:IsA("Hat") then attachAccessory(char, acc:Clone()) end
            end
            local head = char:FindFirstChild("Head")
            if head then
                local face = model:FindFirstChild("face", true)
                if face and face:IsA("Decal") then face:Clone().Parent = head end
            end
            model:Destroy()
            SendNotification("Skin Applied!", 3)
        end)
        
        ResetCharBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            player:LoadCharacter()
        end)
    end

        local function updatePlayerIDs()
            for _, child in pairs(PlayerIDList:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("TextLabel") or child:IsA("TextButton") then child:Destroy() end
            end
            
            local yPos = 0
            for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                local playerEntry = Instance.new("TextButton")
                playerEntry.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 25)
                playerEntry.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, yPos)
                playerEntry.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 30)
                playerEntry.Text = p.Name .. " - ID: " .. tostring(p.UserId)
                playerEntry.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                playerEntry.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                playerEntry.TextSize = 10
                playerEntry.Parent = PlayerIDList
                local entryCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") entryCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3) entryCorner.Parent = playerEntry
                
                playerEntry.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    if setclipboard then setclipboard(tostring(p.UserId)) end
                    SendNotification("Copied: " .. p.Name .. " (" .. tostring(p.UserId) .. ")", 2)
                end)
                
                yPos = yPos + 27
            end
        end
        
        -- Update player list every 2 seconds
        task.spawn(function()
            while true do
                updatePlayerIDs()
                task.wait(2)
            end
        end)
    end

        local colors = {
            Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0), Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0), 
            Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0), Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 255), Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0), 
            Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 255), Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 255), Color3.fromRGB(170, 0, 255)
        }
        
        for _, col in pairs(colors) do
            local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
            btn.Text = ""
            btn.BackgroundColor3 = col
            btn.Parent = ColorFrame
            local c = Instance.new("UICorner") c.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1,0) c.Parent = btn
            
            local stroke = Instance.new("UIStroke")
            stroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(80, 80, 80)
            stroke.Thickness = 1
            stroke.Parent = btn

            btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                Config.ToolColor = col
            end)
        end
    end

        local ChairBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")

        ChairBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 0)
        ChairBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        ChairBtn.Text = "Create Chair"
        ChairBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        ChairBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        ChairBtn.TextSize = 10
        ChairBtn.LayoutOrder = 51
        ChairBtn.Parent = Pages.Visuals
        local ChairCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") ChairCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) ChairCorner.Parent = ChairBtn
        local ChairStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") ChairStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(60, 60, 70) ChairStroke.Thickness = 1 ChairStroke.Parent = ChairBtn
        
        ChairBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local char = player.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                local hrp = char.HumanoidRootPart

                local seat = Instance.new("Seat")
                seat.Name = "CreatedChair"
                seat.Size = Vector3.new(4, 1, 4)
                seat.CFrame = hrp.CFrame + (hrp.CFrame.LookVector * 5)
                seat.Anchored = true
                seat.CanCollide = true
                seat.Transparency = 0.5
                seat.Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 200)
                seat.Parent = workspace

                local clickDetector = Instance.new("ClickDetector")
                clickDetector.MaxActivationDistance = 20
                clickDetector.Parent = seat

                clickDetector.MouseClick:Connect(function(playerWhoClicked)
                    if playerWhoClicked == player then
                        local currentHum = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                        if currentHum then
                            currentHum:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
                            currentHum:Sit(seat)
                        end
                    end
                end)

                SendNotification("Chair created! Click to sit on it.", 3)
            end
        end)
    end

    local FilterModeBtn = createCycle(Pages.Aim, "Filter Mode", "AimFilterMode", {"Whitelist", "Blacklist"}, 11)
    
    do
        local ListFrame = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame")
        ListFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 120)
        ListFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        ListFrame.LayoutOrder = 12
        ListFrame.Parent = Pages.Aim
        
        local UIList = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
        UIList.SortOrder = Enum.SortOrder.Name
        UIList.Parent = ListFrame
        
        local function RefreshFilterList()
            for _, v in pairs(ListFrame:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("TextButton") then v:Destroy() end end
            
            for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if p ~= player then
                    local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                    btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
                    btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                    
                    local status = Config.AimFilterList[p.Name]
                    if status == "Whitelist" then
                        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 150, 0) -- Vert
                    elseif status == "Blacklist" then
                        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 0, 0) -- Rouge
                    else
                        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) -- Gris
                    end
                    
                    btn.Text = p.DisplayName .. " (@" .. p.Name .. ")"
                    btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    btn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                    btn.TextSize = 9
                    btn.Name = p.Name
                    btn.Parent = ListFrame
                    
                    local corner = Instance.new("UICorner") corner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) corner.Parent = btn
                    
                    btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                        local currentStatus = Config.AimFilterList[p.Name]
                        
                        if Config.AimFilterMode == "Whitelist" then
                            if currentStatus == "Whitelist" then
                                Config.AimFilterList[p.Name] = nil
                                btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                            else
                                Config.AimFilterList[p.Name] = "Whitelist"
                                btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 150, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            if currentStatus == "Blacklist" then
                                Config.AimFilterList[p.Name] = nil
                                btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                            else
                                Config.AimFilterList[p.Name] = "Blacklist"
                                btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 0, 0)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
        end
        
        local RefreshBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        RefreshBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
        RefreshBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
        RefreshBtn.Text = "REFRESH PLAYER LIST"
        RefreshBtn.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
        RefreshBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        RefreshBtn.TextSize = 9
        RefreshBtn.LayoutOrder = 13
        RefreshBtn.Parent = Pages.Aim
        local RCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") RCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) RCorner.Parent = RefreshBtn
        
        RefreshBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(RefreshFilterList)
        FilterModeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(RefreshFilterList)
        RefreshFilterList()
    end
