    -- Player Teleport Options (no category)
    local currentTeleportThread = nil
    local currentTeleportTween = nil
    
    local function stopTeleport()
        if currentTeleportThread then
            task.cancel(currentTeleportThread)
            currentTeleportThread = nil
        end
        if currentTeleportTween then
            currentTeleportTween:Cancel()
            currentTeleportTween = nil
        end
        if character and rootPart then
            for _, v in pairs(rootPart:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("BodyVelocity") then v:Destroy() end
            end
        end

        if isOneShotActive then
            isOneShotActive = false
            if oneShotThread then
                task.cancel(oneShotThread)
                oneShotThread = nil
            end
        end
    end

        StopFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)

        StopFrame.Parent = Pages.Teleport

        local StopCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
        StopCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3)
        StopCorner.Parent = StopFrame
        
        local StopBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        StopBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
        StopBtn.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        StopBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
        StopBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        StopBtn.TextSize = 9
        StopBtn.Text = "STOP TELEPORT"
        StopBtn.Parent = StopFrame
        StopBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(stopTeleport)
    end

        if character and rootPart then
            stopTeleport()
            currentTeleportThread = task.spawn(function()
                rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-289.14, 304.96, 592.69)
                task.wait(1)
                
                -- 2. Position de dÃ©part du Fly
                local startPos = Vector3.new(2284.81, 14.25, 899.30)
                local endPos = Vector3.new(4546.18, 53.81, 2711.85)
                
                if character and rootPart then
                    rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(startPos)
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
                
                -- 3. Fly vers la destination (Tween)
                if character and rootPart then
                    local dist = (endPos - startPos).Magnitude
                    local speed = 275 -- Vitesse modÃ©rÃ©e pour Ã©viter le rollback
                    local duration = dist / speed
                    
                    -- Setup Anti-Gravity
                    local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                    bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                    bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
                    bv.Parent = rootPart
                    
                    local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                    local tween = TweenService:Create(rootPart, tweenInfo, {CFrame = CFrame.new(endPos)})
                    currentTeleportTween = tween
                    
                    tween:Play()
                    tween.Completed:Wait()
                    currentTeleportTween = nil
                    
                    if bv then bv:Destroy() end
                end
                currentTeleportThread = nil
            end)
        end
    end)
    end

    createSection(Pages.FarmStatus, "Status", 0.05)
    
    do
        local StatusFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
        StatusFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 120)
        StatusFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        StatusFrame.LayoutOrder = 0.06
        StatusFrame.Parent = Pages.FarmStatus
        
        local UIList = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
        UIList.Parent = StatusFrame
        UIList.Padding = UDim.new(0, 2)
        
        local function createStatusLabel(text)
            local l = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            l.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 15)
            l.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            l.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
            l.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
            l.TextSize = 10
            l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
            l.Text = text
            l.Parent = StatusFrame
            return l
        end
        
        local DimLabel = createStatusLabel("Dimension: ?")
        local BoneLabel = createStatusLabel("Bones: ?")
        local EliteLabel = createStatusLabel("Elite: ?")
        local MirageLabel = createStatusLabel("Mirage: ?")
        local KitsuneLabel = createStatusLabel("Kitsune: ?")
        local MoonLabel = createStatusLabel("Moon: ?")
        local SwordLabel = createStatusLabel("Legendary Sword: ?")
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while Config.IsRunning do
                pcall(function()
                    -- Dimension
                    local dim = "None"
                    local cakeSpawner = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CakePrinceSpawner", true)
                    if cakeSpawner then
                        local count = string.match(cakeSpawner, "%d+")
                        if count then dim = "Need More: " .. count
                        elseif string.find(cakeSpawner, "Do you want to open") then dim = "Ready!" end
                    end
                    DimLabel.Text = "A Dimension: " .. dim
                    
                    -- Bones
                    local bones = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones", "Check") or 0
                    BoneLabel.Text = "Bone You Have: " .. bones
                    
                    -- Elite
                    local elite = "ðŸ”´"
                    if game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Diablo") or game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Deandre") or game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Urban") or workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Diablo") or workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Deandre") or workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Urban") then
                        elite = "ðŸŸ¢"
                    end
                    EliteLabel.Text = "Elite: " .. elite
                    
                    -- Mirage
                    local mirage = "ðŸ”´"
                    if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island") then mirage = "ðŸŸ¢" end
                    MirageLabel.Text = "Mirage Island: " .. mirage
                    
                    -- Kitsune
                    local kitsune = "ðŸ”´"
                    if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island") then kitsune = "ðŸŸ¢" end
                    KitsuneLabel.Text = "Kitsune Island: " .. kitsune
                    
                    -- Moon
                    local moonTxt = "No Full Moon"
                    local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
                    local moonId = (game.PlaceId == 2753915549 or game.PlaceId == 4442272183) and lighting.FantasySky.MoonTextureId or lighting.Sky.MoonTextureId
                    if moonId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149431" or moonId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=4303207962" then moonTxt = "Full Moon"
                    elseif moonId == "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149052" then moonTxt = "Next Night" end
                    MoonLabel.Text = "Moon: " .. moonTxt
                    
                    -- Legendary Sword
                    local sword = "ðŸ”´"
                    if game.PlaceId == 4442272183 then
                        local sData = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LegendarySwordDealer", "1")
                        if sData and sData ~= "1" then sword = sData end
                    end
                    SwordLabel.Text = "Legendary Sword: " .. sword
                end)
                task.wait(1)
            end
        end)
    end

    createSection(Pages.FarmFarming, "Farming", 0.07)
    
    -- Move Farm Nearest Here
    createToggle(Pages.FarmFarming, "Enable Farm Nearest", "CustomFarmNearest", 0.08)
    
    -- Move Mastery Farm Here

    -- Auto Farm Elite
    createToggle(Pages.FarmFarming, "Auto Farm Elite", "AutoElitehunter", 0.10)

    -- Forward declaration for Fast M1
    local StartFastM1, FastM1Btn
    
    task.spawn(function()
        local function TweenToElite(targetPos)
            if not rootPart then return end
            local dist = (rootPart.Position - targetPos).Magnitude
            if dist < 25 then return end
            
            local speed = 400
            local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
            local tween = TweenService:Create(rootPart, info, {CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)})
            
            local noclipConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                if character then
                    for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                    end
                end
            end)
            
            tween:Play()
            
            while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                if not Config.IsRunning or not Config.AutoElitehunter then tween:Cancel() break end
                if not rootPart or (humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0) then tween:Cancel() break end
                task.wait(0.03)
            end
            
            if noclipConn then noclipConn:Disconnect() end
            if rootPart then rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) end
        end

        -- Function to equip melee weapon
        local function EquipMeleeWeapon()
            if not player.Character or not player:FindFirstChild("Backpack") or not player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then return end
            local backpack = player.Backpack
            local humanoid = player.Character.Humanoid
            
            -- Find melee weapons (swords, blades, katanas, etc.)
            local meleeKeywords = {"sword", "blade", "katana", "saber", "cutlass", "pole", "spear", "trident"}
            
            for _, tool in pairs(backpack:GetChildren()) do
                if tool:IsA("Tool") then
                    local toolName = tool.Name:lower()
                    for _, keyword in pairs(meleeKeywords) do
                        if string.find(toolName, keyword) then
                            humanoid:EquipTool(tool)
                            return true
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            
            -- If no keyword match, equip any tool
            local anyTool = backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
            if anyTool then
                humanoid:EquipTool(anyTool)
                return true
            end
            
            return false
        end

        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.AutoElitehunter then
                -- Auto Enable Fast M1
                if not Config.FastM1 then
                    Config.FastM1 = true
                    if FastM1Btn then
                        FastM1Btn.Text = "STOP FAST M1"
                        FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                    end
                    if StartFastM1 then StartFastM1() end
                end

                pcall(function()
                    -- Get quest
                    local questGui = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui") and player.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("Main") and player.PlayerGui.Main:FindFirstChild("Quest")
                    if not questGui or not questGui.Visible then
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("EliteHunter")
                        task.wait(0.5)
                    else
                        local questLabel = questGui:FindFirstChild("Container") and questGui.Container:FindFirstChild("QuestTitle") and questGui.Container.QuestTitle:FindFirstChild("Title")
                        if questLabel and questLabel.Text then
                            if string.find(questLabel.Text, "Diablo") or string.find(questLabel.Text, "Deandre") or string.find(questLabel.Text, "Urban") then
                                local targetName = ""
                                if string.find(questLabel.Text, "Diablo") then targetName = "Diablo" end
                                if string.find(questLabel.Text, "Deandre") then targetName = "Deandre" end
                                if string.find(questLabel.Text, "Urban") then targetName = "Urban" end
                                
                                -- Ensure melee weapon is equipped
                                EquipMeleeWeapon()
                                
                                -- Search for elite
                                local target = workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(targetName)
                                
                                if not target or not target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    -- Check ReplicatedStorage
                                    local storageTarget = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild(targetName)
                                    if storageTarget and storageTarget:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        TweenToElite(storageTarget.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
                                    else
                                        task.wait(0.5)
                                    end
                                else
                                    -- Elite found, stay ABOVE and attack
                                    while Config.AutoElitehunter and target and target:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and target.Humanoid.Health > 0 and target.Parent do
                                        pcall(function()
                                            EquipMeleeWeapon()
                                            
                                            if target.Parent == workspace.Enemies then
                                                -- Stay ABOVE the elite and attack
                                                if rootPart and target.HumanoidRootPart then
                                                    rootPart.CFrame = target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 25, 0)
                                                    rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                                                end
                                                
                                                -- Reduce hitbox for easier hitting
                                                if target.HumanoidRootPart then
                                                    target.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 2)
                                                    target.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
                                                end
                                                
                                                -- Rapid click attack
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(camera.ViewportSize.X/2, camera.ViewportSize.Y/2, 0, true, game, 1)
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(camera.ViewportSize.X/2, camera.ViewportSize.Y/2, 0, false, game, 1)
                                            else
                                                -- Elite spawned elsewhere, go to it
                                                local newTarget = workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(targetName)
                                                if newTarget and newTarget:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                                    target = newTarget
                                                    TweenToElite(target.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
                                                end
                                            end
                                        end)
                                        task.wait(0.05)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end)

    createSection(Pages.FarmSettings, "Settings", 0.5)

    createCycle(Pages.FarmSettings, "Select Weapon", "SelectWeaponType", {"Melee", "Sword", "Blox Fruit"}, 0.55)
    
    createToggle(Pages.FarmSettings, "Bring Mob", "BringMob", 0.56)
    
    createSlider(Pages.FarmSettings, "Bring Range", "BringRange", 0.57, 50, 500, 50)
    
    createToggle(Pages.FarmSettings, "Fast M1 (Auto)", "FastM1Auto", 0.57)

    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            task.wait(1)
            pcall(function()
                local desiredType = Config.SelectWeaponType
                local foundWeapon = nil
                
                local function isMatch(tool)
                    return tool:IsA("Tool") and tool.ToolTip == desiredType
                end
                
                if player.Character then
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Character:GetChildren()) do
                        if isMatch(t) then foundWeapon = t.Name break end
                    end
                end
                
                if not foundWeapon and player.Backpack then
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
                        if isMatch(t) then foundWeapon = t.Name break end
                    end
                end
                
                if foundWeapon then Config.SelectedWeapon = foundWeapon end
            end)
        end
    end)

    do
        local FastM1Btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        FastM1Btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        FastM1Btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        FastM1Btn.Text = "Op Fast M1" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
        FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        FastM1Btn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        FastM1Btn.TextSize = 10
        FastM1Btn.LayoutOrder = 0.6
        FastM1Btn.Parent = Pages.FarmSettings
        local c = Instance.new("UICorner") c.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,4) c.Parent = FastM1Btn
        
        StartFastM1 = function()
            task.spawn(function()
                local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local Net = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Modules", 10) and ReplicatedStorage.Modules:WaitForChild("Net", 10)
                
                if not Net then
                    SendNotification("Net Module not found (Not Blox Fruits?)", 3)
                    Config.FastM1 = false
                    FastM1Btn.Text = "Op Fast M1" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
                    FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    return
                end
                
                local RegisterHit = Net:WaitForChild("RE/RegisterHit", 5)
                local RegisterAttack = Net:WaitForChild("RE/RegisterAttack", 5)

                local function AttackMultipleTargets(targets)
                    pcall(function()
                        if not targets or #targets == 0 then return end
                        local allTargets = {}
                        for _, targetChar in pairs(targets) do
                            local head = targetChar:FindFirstChild("Head")
                            local torso = targetChar:FindFirstChild("Torso") or targetChar:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
                            local hrp = targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if head then table.insert(allTargets, {targetChar, head}) end
                            if torso and torso ~= head then table.insert(allTargets, {targetChar, torso}) end
                            if hrp and hrp ~= head and hrp ~= torso then table.insert(allTargets, {targetChar, hrp}) end
                        end
                        if #allTargets == 0 then return end
                        for i = 1, 3 do
                            RegisterAttack:FireServer(0)
                            RegisterHit:FireServer(allTargets[1][2], allTargets)
                        end
                    end)
                end

               while Config.FastM1 and Config.IsRunning do
                    task.wait(0.01)
                    local myChar = player.Character
                    local myHRP = myChar and myChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    
                    if myHRP then
                        local targetsInRange = {}
                        local enemiesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies")
                        if enemiesFolder then
                            for _, npc in pairs(enemiesFolder:GetChildren()) do
                                local humanoid = npc:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                local hrp = npc:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if humanoid and hrp and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                    if (hrp.Position - myHRP.Position).Magnitude <= 5000 then
                                        table.insert(targetsInRange, npc)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if p ~= player and p.Character then
                                local humanoid = p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                local hrp = p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if humanoid and hrp and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                    if (hrp.Position - myHRP.Position).Magnitude <= 5000 then
                                        table.insert(targetsInRange, p.Character)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        if #targetsInRange > 0 then AttackMultipleTargets(targetsInRange) end
                    end
                end
                
                if not Config.FastM1 and FastM1Btn then
                    FastM1Btn.Text = "Op Fast M1" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
                    FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                end
            end)
        end

        FastM1Btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if not Config.IsWhitelisted then SendNotification("Your key is not whitelisted, you cannot use this option", 3) return end
            
            Config.FastM1 = not Config.FastM1
            
            if Config.FastM1 then
                FastM1Btn.Text = "STOP FAST M1"
                FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                StartFastM1()
            else
                FastM1Btn.Text = "Op Fast M1" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
                FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            end
        end)
    end



    -- Hook Farm Toggles to Fast M1
    local function UpdateFastM1State()
        local shouldBeOn = Config.CustomFarmNearest or Config.MasteryFarm or Config.AutoElitehunter
        if shouldBeOn and not Config.FastM1 then
            Config.FastM1 = true
            if FastM1Btn then
                FastM1Btn.Text = "STOP FAST M1"
                FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            end
            if StartFastM1 then StartFastM1() end
        elseif not shouldBeOn and Config.FastM1 then
             Config.FastM1 = false
             if FastM1Btn then
                FastM1Btn.Text = "Op Fast M1" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
                FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
             end
        end
    end

    if ToggleButtons["CustomFarmNearest"] then ToggleButtons["CustomFarmNearest"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(UpdateFastM1State) end
    if ToggleButtons["MasteryFarm"] then ToggleButtons["MasteryFarm"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(UpdateFastM1State) end
    if ToggleButtons["AutoElitehunter"] then ToggleButtons["AutoElitehunter"].MouseButton1Click:Connect(UpdateFastM1State) end

        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(remoteArg)
        end)
    end

            local function StopAutoFarm()
                _G.AutoFarm = false; _G.CurrentQuestData = nil
                local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    char.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
                    char.HumanoidRootPart.Transparency = 1
                    char.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = true
                end
                local cx, cy = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.X / 2, workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.Y / 2
                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 1, false, game, 1)
                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 0, false, game, 1)
            end

            UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, processed)
                if not processed and StopAllKey and input.KeyCode == StopAllKey then
                    StopAutoFarm()
                end
            end)

            local LastTargetTime = 0
            task.spawn(function()
                while task.wait() do
                    if _G.AutoFarm and _G.CurrentQuestData then
                        pcall(function()
                            local char = LocalPlayer.Character
                            local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local target = nil
                                local minDist = 3000
                                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == _G.CurrentQuestData.Mob and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                        local dist = (hrp.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                        if dist < minDist then
                                            minDist = dist
                                            target = v
                                        end
                                    end
                                end

                                local backpack = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                                local tool = char:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool")
                                if not tool and backpack then
                                    for _, item in pairs(backpack:GetChildren()) do
                                        if item:IsA("Tool") then
                                            char.Humanoid:EquipTool(item)
                                            tool = item
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                end

                                if target then
                                    LastTargetTime = os.clock()
                                    hrp.Size = Vector3.new(25, 25, 25)
                                    hrp.Transparency = 1
                                    hrp.CanCollide = false

                                    local targetHRP = target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetHRP then
                                        hrp.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)

                                        if (hrp.Position - targetHRP.Position).Magnitude < 30 then
                                            local isOverUI = false
                                            pcall(function()
                                                local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
                                                local objects = PlayerGui:GetGuiObjectsAtPosition(mousePos.X, mousePos.Y)
                                                for _, obj in pairs(objects) do
                                                    if obj:IsDescendantOf(ScreenGui) or (GalaxyHubGui and obj:IsDescendantOf(GalaxyHubGui)) then
                                                        isOverUI = true; break
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end)

                                            local cx, cy = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.X / 2, workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize.Y / 2

                                            if not isOverUI then
                                                if tool then tool:Activate() end
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 1, true, game, 1)
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 0, true, game, 1)
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 0, false, game, 1)
                                            else
                                                VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(cx, cy, 1, false, game, 1)
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                    hrp.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                else
                                    if _G.CurrentQuestData.Spawn then
                                        local spawnPos = _G.CurrentQuestData.Spawn
                                        local distToSpawn = (hrp.Position - spawnPos).Magnitude
                                        
                                        if distToSpawn > 150 then
                                            local dir = (spawnPos - hrp.Position).Unit
                                            local step = math.min(distToSpawn, 200)
                                            local targetPos = hrp.Position + (dir * step)
                                            local ti = TweenInfo.new(step / 350, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                                            local tw = TweenService:Create(hrp, ti, {CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)})
                                            tw:Play()
                                            tw.Completed:Wait()
                                            for _, v in pairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
                                                if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                                            end
                                        else
                                            hrp.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                        end
                                    else
                                        hrp.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    else
                        LastTargetTime = os.clock()
                    end
                end
            end)

            if GalaxyHubGui then
                GalaxyHubGui:Destroy()
                GalaxyHubGui = nil
            else
                local targetGui = (gethui and gethui()) or game:GetService("CoreGui")
                GalaxyHubGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui", targetGui)
                GalaxyHubGui.Name = "Ton618UI"
                
                local Main = Instance.new("Frame", GalaxyHubGui)
                Main.Size = UDim2.new(0, 480, 0, 520)
                Main.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -240, 0.5, -260)
                Main.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(12, 12, 12)
                Main.BorderSizePixel = 0
                Main.Active = true
                Main.Draggable = true
                
                local MainCorner = Instance.new("UICorner", Main) MainCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 2)
                local MainStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", Main) MainStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(45, 45, 45) MainStroke.Thickness = 1
                
                local TitleFrame = Instance.new("Frame", Main)
                TitleFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 120, 0, 32)
                TitleFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, 15)
                TitleFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(12, 12, 12)
                TitleFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
                
                local TitleText = Instance.new("TextLabel", TitleFrame)
                TitleText.Text = "TON 618"
                TitleText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                TitleText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                TitleText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                TitleText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBlack
                TitleText.TextSize = 16

                local CloseBtn = Instance.new("TextButton", Main)
                CloseBtn.Text = "X"
                CloseBtn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                CloseBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
                CloseBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 20)
                CloseBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 30, 0, 30)
                CloseBtn.Position = UDim2.new(1, -45, 0, 15)
                CloseBtn.TextSize = 14
                local CloseCorner = Instance.new("UICorner", CloseBtn) CloseCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 2)
                
                CloseBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    GalaxyHubGui:Destroy()
                    GalaxyHubGui = nil
                end)

                local Content = Instance.new("ScrollingFrame", Main)
                Content.Size = UDim2.new(0.9, 0, 0.75, 0)
                Content.Position = UDim2.new(0.05, 0, 0.15, 0)
                Content.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                Content.ScrollBarThickness = 2
                Content.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
                Content.AutomaticCanvasSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
                local Layout = Instance.new("UIListLayout", Content); Layout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 8)

                local function CreateBtn(text, color, parent)
                    local b = Instance.new("TextButton", parent or Content)
                    b.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 45)
                    b.Text = text
                    b.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 25, 25)
                    b.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                    b.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
                    b.TextSize = 14
                    local bCorner = Instance.new("UICorner", b) bCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 2)
                    local bStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke", b) bStroke.Color = color bStroke.Thickness = 1
                    return b
                end

                local function ClearContent()
                    for _, v in pairs(Content:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("TextButton") then v:Destroy() end end
                end

                local ShowSeaMenu, ShowIslandMenu, ShowQuestMenu

                ShowSeaMenu = function()
                    ClearContent()
                    for _, sea in pairs({"SEA 1", "SEA 2", "SEA 3"}) do
                        CreateBtn(sea, Color3.fromRGB(255, 130, 0)).MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() ShowIslandMenu(sea) end)
                    end
                end

                ShowIslandMenu = function(sea)
                    ClearContent()
                    CreateBtn("â¬… BACK", Color3.fromRGB(200, 50, 50)).MouseButton1Click:Connect(ShowSeaMenu)
                    for _, islandData in ipairs(GameData[sea]) do
                        CreateBtn(islandData.Emoji .. " " .. islandData.Name, islandData.Color).MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() ShowQuestMenu(sea, islandData) end)
                    end
                end

                ShowQuestMenu = function(sea, islandData)
                    ClearContent()
                    CreateBtn("â¬… BACK", Color3.fromRGB(200, 50, 50)).MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() ShowIslandMenu(sea) end)
                    for _, info in pairs(islandData.Mobs) do
                        CreateBtn("âš”ï¸ ["..info.Level.."] "..info.Mob, Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50)).MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            _G.CurrentQuestData = info; _G.AutoFarm = true
                        end)
                    end
                end

                local StopText = StopAllKey and ("ðŸ›‘ STOP ALL [" .. StopAllKey.Name .. "]") or "ðŸ›‘ STOP ALL [NONE]"
                local Stop = CreateBtn(StopText, Color3.fromRGB(200, 0, 0), Main)
                Stop.Position = UDim2.new(0.1, 0, 0.85, 0); Stop.Size = UDim2.new(0.8, 0, 0, 50)
                
                local isBindingStop = false
                Stop.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    isBindingStop = true
                    Stop.Text = "Press a key..."
                end)

                local bindConn = UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
                    if isBindingStop and input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
                        StopAllKey = input.KeyCode
                        isBindingStop = false
                        Stop.Text = "ðŸ›‘ STOP ALL [" .. input.KeyCode.Name .. "]"
                    end
                end)
                
                Main.Destroying:Connect(function()
                    if bindConn then bindConn:Disconnect() end
                end)

                ShowSeaMenu()
            end
        end)
    end)
    end
    
    -- Sea Event Page Content
    createSection(Pages.SeaEvent, "Leviathan", 1)
    createToggle(Pages.SeaEvent, "Auto Find Leviathan", "AutoFindLeviathan", 2)
    
    createSection(Pages.SeaEvent, "Boat Control", 3)
    createToggle(Pages.SeaEvent, "Auto Buy Boat & Sit", "AutoBuyBoat", 4)
    createCycle(Pages.SeaEvent, "Select Boat", "SelectedBoat", {"Speedboat", "Luxury Boat", "Grand Brigade", "Guardian", "Lantern", "Miracle", "Sloop", "Dinghy", "Beast Hunter", "Sleigh"}, 5)
    
    -- Shop Page Content
    local function createBuyBtn(parent, text, args, order, targetInfo)
        local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        btn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 25)
        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
        btn.Text = text
        btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
        btn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
        btn.TextSize = 9
        btn.LayoutOrder = order
        btn.Parent = parent
        local c = Instance.new("UICorner") c.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0,4) c.Parent = btn
        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            local savedCFrame = nil
            if character and rootPart then savedCFrame = rootPart.CFrame end
            
            local targetPos = nil
            
            if typeof(targetInfo) == "Vector3" then
                targetPos = CFrame.new(targetInfo)
            elseif typeof(targetInfo) == "string" then
                local npcName = targetInfo
                local targetNPC = nil
                
                local folders = {
                    workspace:FindFirstChild("NPCs"),
                    workspace:FindFirstChild("Map") and workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("NPCs"),
                    workspace:FindFirstChild("Spawn") and workspace.Spawn:FindFirstChild("NPCs")
                }
                
                for _, f in pairs(folders) do
                    if f then
                        targetNPC = f:FindFirstChild(npcName)
                        if targetNPC then break end
                    end
                end
                
                if not targetNPC then
                    for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v.Name == npcName and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            targetNPC = v
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
                if targetNPC and targetNPC:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    targetPos = targetNPC.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 3)
                end
            end
            
            if targetPos and rootPart then
                local wasAnchored = rootPart.Anchored
                rootPart.Anchored = true
                local startTime = tick()
                while tick() - startTime < 0.5 do
                    if rootPart then 
                        rootPart.CFrame = targetPos 
                        rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                        rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                    end
                    RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                end
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack(args))
                if rootPart then rootPart.Anchored = wasAnchored end
                if savedCFrame then rootPart.CFrame = savedCFrame end
            else
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer(unpack(args))
            end
        end)
    end

    local function UpdateTheme(newColor)
        CurrentThemeColor = newColor
        Title.TextColor3 = newColor
        ExpandButton.TextColor3 = newColor
        
        -- Update Tabs Stroke
        for name, btn in pairs(TabBtns) do
            if Pages[name].Visible then
                btn.UIStroke.Color = newColor
            end
        end
        
        -- Update Hub Buttons
        for _, btn in pairs(HubMenu:GetChildren()) do
            if btn:IsA("TextButton") then
                btn.TextColor3 = newColor
            end
        end
        
        -- Update Patch Notes Button
        if PatchNotesBtn then
            PatchNotesBtn.TextColor3 = newColor
            if PatchNotesBtn:FindFirstChild("UIStroke") then PatchNotesBtn.UIStroke.Color = newColor end
        end
        if PatchNotesPage then
            for _, f in pairs(PatchNotesPage:GetChildren()) do
                local vl = f:FindFirstChild("VersionLabel")
                if vl then vl.TextColor3 = newColor end
            end
        end
        
        -- Update Toggles (Active)
        for key, btn in pairs(ToggleButtons) do
            if Config[key] then
                btn.BackgroundColor3 = newColor
            end
        end
        
        -- Update Inputs & Keybinds Text
        for _, page in pairs(Pages) do
            for _, obj in pairs(page:GetDescendants()) do
                if obj:IsA("TextBox") then
                    obj.TextColor3 = newColor
                elseif obj:IsA("TextButton") and obj.Parent:FindFirstChild("UIStroke") and obj.Text ~= "" and obj.Name ~= "ExpandButton" then
                    -- Heuristic to find Keybind/Input buttons (not toggles which have empty text)
                    obj.TextColor3 = newColor
                end
            end
        end
    end

    createSection(Pages.Settings, "Configuration Manager", 3)
    
    local ConfigFolder = "Cyberpunks_Configs"
    if makefolder then pcall(function() makefolder(ConfigFolder) end) end
    
    local function SaveConfig(name)
        if not writefile then return end
        local jsonConfig = {}
        for k, v in pairs(Config) do
            if typeof(v) == "EnumItem" then
                jsonConfig[k] = {Type = "Enum", Name = v.Name, EnumType = tostring(v.EnumType)}
            elseif typeof(v) == "Color3" then
                jsonConfig[k] = {Type = "Color3", R = v.R, G = v.G, B = v.B}
            else
                jsonConfig[k] = v
            end
        end
        pcall(function() writefile(ConfigFolder .. "/" .. name .. ".json", HttpService:JSONEncode(jsonConfig)) end)
    end

    local function LoadConfig(name)
        if not readfile or not isfile(ConfigFolder .. "/" .. name .. ".json") then return end
        local content = readfile(ConfigFolder .. "/" .. name .. ".json")
        local decoded = HttpService:JSONDecode(content)
        
        for k, v in pairs(decoded) do
            if Config[k] ~= nil then
                if type(v) == "table" and v.Type == "Enum" then
                    local success, val = pcall(function() return Enum[tostring(v.EnumType):match("Enum%.(%w+)")] end)
                    if success and val then
                        Config[k] = val[v.Name]
                    else
                        pcall(function() Config[k] = Enum.KeyCode[v.Name] end)
                    end
                elseif type(v) == "table" and v.Type == "Color3" then
                    Config[k] = Color3.new(v.R, v.G, v.B)
                else
                    Config[k] = v
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Update UI
        for k, btn in pairs(ToggleButtons) do
            btn.BackgroundColor3 = Config[k] and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        end
        for k, btn in pairs(KeybindButtons) do
            local keyName = Config[k].Name
            if Config[k] == Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then keyName = "..." end
            btn.Text = keyName
        end
        for k, input in pairs(InputBoxes) do
            input.Text = tostring(Config[k])
        end
        
        if _G.SnowGui then
            _G.SnowGui.Enabled = not Config.DisableSnow
        end
        
        UpdateTheme(CurrentThemeColor)
        
        -- Apply Cursor
        if Config.CustomCursorId and Config.CustomCursorId ~= "" then
             local val = Config.CustomCursorId
             if tonumber(val) then
                mouse.Icon = "rbxassetid://" .. val
             else
                mouse.Icon = val
             end
        end
        
        -- Apply FastM1 if enabled in config
        if Config.FastM1 and Config.IsWhitelisted then
            if FastM1Btn then
                FastM1Btn.Text = "STOP FAST M1"
                FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            end
            if StartFastM1 then StartFastM1() end
        end
        
        -- Apply Infinite Zoom if enabled in config
        if Config.InfiniteZoom then
            player.CameraMaxZoomDistance = 100000
            player.CameraMinZoomDistance = 0.5
        end
    end

    do

    local function RefreshConfigs()
        for _, v in pairs(ListFrame:GetChildren()) do if v:IsA("Frame") or v:IsA("TextButton") then v:Destroy() end end
        if listfiles then
            pcall(function()
                for _, file in pairs(listfiles(ConfigFolder)) do
                    local name = file:match("([^\\/]+)%.json$")
                    if name then
                        local Row = Instance.new("Frame")
                        Row.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 20)
                        Row.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                        Row.Parent = ListFrame
                        
                        local btn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                        btn.Size = UDim2.new(0.8, 0, 1, 0)
                        btn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 40)
                        btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
                        btn.Text = name
                        btn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                        btn.TextSize = 9
                        btn.Parent = Row
                        
                        local BCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") BCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) BCorner.Parent = btn
                        
                        btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            LoadConfig(name)
                        end)
                        
                        local delBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
                        delBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0.15, 0, 1, 0)
                        delBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0.85, 0, 0, 0)
                        delBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
                        delBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                        delBtn.Text = "ðŸ—‘"
                        delBtn.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham
                        delBtn.TextSize = 10
                        delBtn.Parent = Row
                        
                        local DCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") DCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) DCorner.Parent = delBtn
                        
                        delBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            if delfile then
                                pcall(function() delfile(file) end)
                                Row:Destroy()
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end)
        end
    end
    
    SaveBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if CFName.Text ~= "" then
            SaveConfig(CFName.Text)
            CFName.Text = ""
            task.wait(0.2)
            RefreshConfigs()
        end
    end)
    
    RefreshConfigs()
    end
    
    -- Auto Load Script Button (loads Cyberpunks.lua from GitHub)
    do

                local savedAutoLoad = data.Enabled

                if savedConfigName then
                    Config.AutoLoadConfigName = savedConfigName
                    if InputBoxes["AutoLoadConfigName"] then InputBoxes["AutoLoadConfigName"].Text = savedConfigName end
                end
                
                if savedAutoLoad ~= nil then
                    Config.AutoLoadConfig = savedAutoLoad
                    if ToggleButtons["AutoLoadConfig"] then 
                        ToggleButtons["AutoLoadConfig"].BackgroundColor3 = savedAutoLoad and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)

                        Config.AutoLoadConfigName = savedConfigName

                    end

                end
            end
        end)

    -- Removed Farm Nearest from Custom (Moved to FarmScripts)
    -- createSection(Pages.Custom, "Farm Nearest (OP)", 3)
    -- createToggle(Pages.Custom, "Enable Farm Nearest", "CustomFarmNearest", 3.1)
    
    task.spawn(function()
        local function TweenTo(targetPos)
            if character and rootPart and rootPart.Parent then
                local dist = (rootPart.Position - targetPos).Magnitude
                if dist < 5 then return end
                
                local speed = 300 
                local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local tween = TweenService:Create(rootPart, info, {CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)})
                
                local noclipConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                    if character then
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                tween:Play()
                
                while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                    if not Config.IsRunning or not Config.CustomFarmNearest then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    if not character or not rootPart or not rootPart.Parent or (humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0) then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    if (rootPart.Position - targetPos).Magnitude < 5 then
                         tween:Cancel()
                         break
                    end
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
                
                if noclipConn then noclipConn:Disconnect() end
                if rootPart then rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) end
            end
        end

        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.CustomFarmNearest and character and rootPart then
                if not Config.FastM1 then
                    -- Config.FastM1 = true
                    -- if FastM1Btn then
                    --     FastM1Btn.Text = "STOP FAST M1"
                    --     FastM1Btn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                    -- end
                    -- if StartFastM1 then StartFastM1() end
                end
                
                local target = nil
                local minDist = 99999
                
                local function scan(folder)
                    for _, v in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
                        if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local dist = (rootPart.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            if dist < minDist then
                                minDist = dist
                                target = v
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies") then scan(workspace.Enemies) end
                scan(workspace)
                
                if target then
                    local targetPos = target.HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 15, 0)
                    local currentPos = rootPart.Position
                    local dist = (currentPos - targetPos).Magnitude
                    
                    if dist > 15 then
                        TweenTo(targetPos)
                    else
                        rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos, target.HumanoidRootPart.Position)
                        rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                    end
                    
                    for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.05)
        end
    end)

    -- Removed Mastery Farm from Custom (Moved to FarmScripts)

    -- Player Finder (Moved from Shop)
    createSection(Pages.Custom, "Player Finder (Whitelist)", 3)
    createInput(Pages.Custom, "Username", "JoinPlayerName", 3.1)
    
    do
        local FinderBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        FinderBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        FinderBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        FinderBtn.Text = "FIND PLAYER (BOT LINK)" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
        FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        FinderBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        FinderBtn.TextSize = 10
        FinderBtn.LayoutOrder = 3.2
        FinderBtn.Parent = Pages.Custom
        
        local FCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") FCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) FCorner.Parent = FinderBtn
        
        local isFinding = false

        FinderBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if not Config.IsWhitelisted then
                SendNotification("Whitelist required for Player Finder!", 3)
                return
            end

            if isFinding then
                isFinding = false
                FinderBtn.Text = "FIND PLAYER (BOT LINK)"
                FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                SendNotification("Bot search stopped.", 2)
                return
            end

            local username = Config.JoinPlayerName
            if not username or username == "" then
                SendNotification("Please enter a username.", 3)
                return
            end
            
            local apiUrl = Config.BotApiUrl
            if not apiUrl or apiUrl == "" then
                SendNotification("Please enter your Bot API URL.", 3)
                return
            end
            
            isFinding = true
            FinderBtn.Text = "STOP BOT SEARCH"
            FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            
            local requestFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or (fluxus and fluxus.request) or request
            if not requestFunc then
                SendNotification("Executor does not support HTTP requests.", 4)
                isFinding = false
                return
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                -- 1. Send Search Request to Bot
                SendNotification("Sending request to Bot...", 2)
                local success, response = pcall(function()
                    return requestFunc({
                        Url = apiUrl .. "/search",
                        Method = "POST",
                        Headers = {["Content-Type"] = "application/json"},
                        Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({username = username})
                    })
                end)
                
                if not success or not response or response.StatusCode ~= 200 then
                    SendNotification("Failed to contact Bot.", 3)
                    isFinding = false
                    FinderBtn.Text = "FIND PLAYER (BOT LINK)"
                    FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    return
                end
                
                SendNotification("Bot is searching for " .. username .. "...", 3)
                
                -- 2. Poll for Status
                while isFinding and Config.IsRunning do
                    local pSuccess, pResponse = pcall(function()
                        return requestFunc({
                            Url = apiUrl .. "/status?username=" .. username,
                            Method = "GET"
                        })
                    end)
                    
                    if pSuccess and pResponse and pResponse.StatusCode == 200 then
                        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(pResponse.Body)
                        if data.status == "found" and data.jobId then
                            if data.jobId == game.JobId then
                                SendNotification("You are already in the correct server!", 5)
                                isFinding = false
                                FinderBtn.Text = "FIND PLAYER (BOT LINK)"
                                FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                                break
                            end
                            
                            isFinding = false
                            FinderBtn.Text = "FIND PLAYER (BOT LINK)"
                            FinderBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                            
                            local targetPlaceId = data.placeId or game.PlaceId
                            CreateConfirmationPrompt("Player Found!\nServer ID: " .. data.jobId, data.jobId, targetPlaceId, function()
                                local success, err = pcall(function()
                                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(targetPlaceId, tostring(data.jobId), player)
                                end)
                                if not success then SendNotification("Teleport failed. Please retry.", 4) end
                            end, function()
                                SendNotification("Join cancelled.", 3)
                            end)
                            
                            break
                        elseif data.status == "error" then
                            SendNotification("Bot Error: " .. (data.message or "Unknown"), 3)
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(3) -- Poll every 3 seconds
                end
            end)
        end)

    end

    do
        local ScannerBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
        ScannerBtn.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 30)
        ScannerBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 20, 25)
        ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)" .. (Config.IsWhitelisted and "" or " ðŸ”’")
        ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        ScannerBtn.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
        ScannerBtn.TextSize = 10
        ScannerBtn.LayoutOrder = 3.3
        ScannerBtn.Parent = Pages.Custom
        
        local SCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") SCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) SCorner.Parent = ScannerBtn
        
        local isScanning = false

        ScannerBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            if not Config.IsWhitelisted then
                SendNotification("Whitelist required for Player Finder!", 3)
                return
            end

            if isScanning then
                isScanning = false
                ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)"
                ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                SendNotification("Scanner stopped.", 2)
                return
            end

            local username = Config.JoinPlayerName
            if not username or username == "" then
                SendNotification("Please enter a username.", 3)
                return
            end
            
            local requestFunc = (syn and syn.request) or (http and http.request) or http_request or (fluxus and fluxus.request) or request
            if not requestFunc then
                SendNotification("Executor does not support HTTP requests.", 4)
                return
            end
            
            isScanning = true
            ScannerBtn.Text = "STOP SCANNING"
            ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            
            task.spawn(function()
                -- 1. Get User ID
                local userId
                local uSuccess = pcall(function() userId = Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(username) end)
                if not uSuccess or not userId then
                    SendNotification("User not found.", 3)
                    isScanning = false
                    ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)"
                    ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    return
                end
                
                SendNotification("Fetching target thumbnails...", 2)
                
                -- 2. Get Target Thumbnail Hash (OPTIMIZED & RESILIENT)
                local targetHash = ""
                local function getThumbHash(uId)
                    local urls = {
                        "https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/users/avatar-headshot?userIds=" .. uId .. "&size=48x48&format=Png&isCircular=false",
                        "https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/users/avatar-bust?userIds=" .. uId .. "&size=48x48&format=Png&isCircular=false"
                    }
                    
                    for _, url in pairs(urls) do
                        -- Try 1: game:HttpGet (Standard)
                        local s, body = pcall(function() return game:HttpGet(url) end)
                        
                        -- Try 2: request with Cookie if HttpGet failed
                        if (not s or not body) and requestFunc then
                            local rS, rR = pcall(function()
                                return requestFunc({
                                    Url = url,
                                    Method = "GET",
                                    Headers = {}
                                })
                            end)
                            if rS and rR.StatusCode == 200 then body = rR.Body end
                        end
                        
                        if body then
                            local d = HttpService:JSONDecode(body)
                            if d and d.data and d.data[1] and d.data[1].imageUrl then
                                local hash = d.data[1].imageUrl:match("rbxcdn%.com/([%w%-]+)")
                                if hash then return hash end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    return nil
                end

                targetHash = getThumbHash(userId)
                
                if not targetHash then
                    SendNotification("Failed to get player thumbnail.", 3)
                    isScanning = false
                    ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)"
                    ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                    return
                end

                SendNotification("Deep scanning all Seas...", 3)
                
                local bfSeas = {2753915549, 4442272183, 7449423635}
                local placesToScan = {game.PlaceId}
                local isBF = false
                for _, id in pairs(bfSeas) do if game.PlaceId == id then isBF = true break end end
                if isBF then placesToScan = bfSeas end

                for _, placeId in pairs(placesToScan) do
                    if not isScanning or not Config.IsRunning then break end
                    
                    local seaName = (placeId == 2753915549 and "Sea 1") or (placeId == 4442272183 and "Sea 2") or (placeId == 7449423635 and "Sea 3") or "Game"
                    SendNotification("Deep Scan: " .. seaName .. "...", 2)
                    
                    local cursor = ""
                    local serversChecked = 0
                    
                    while isScanning and Config.IsRunning and cursor ~= nil do
                        -- Utilisation de game:HttpGet pour utiliser la session actuelle (Cookie)
                        local sSuccess, sBody = pcall(function()
                            return game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?limit=100&cursor=" .. (cursor or ""))
                        end)
                        
                        if not sSuccess or not sBody then 
                            -- Fallback vers request si HttpGet Ã©choue
                            local rS, rR = pcall(function()
                                return requestFunc({
                                    Url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?limit=100&cursor=" .. (cursor or ""),
                                    Method = "GET",
                                    Headers = {}
                                })
                            end)
                            if rS and rR.StatusCode == 200 then sBody = rR.Body else break end
                        end

                        local sData = HttpService:JSONDecode(sBody)
                        if not sData or not sData.data then break end
                        cursor = sData.nextPageCursor
                        
                        local currentBatch = {}
                        local serverMap = {}
                        
                        for _, server in pairs(sData.data) do
                            if not isScanning or not Config.IsRunning then break end
                            if server.playerTokens then
                                for _, token in pairs(server.playerTokens) do
                                    table.insert(currentBatch, {
                                        requestId = token,
                                        type = "AvatarHeadShot",
                                        token = token,
                                        size = "48x48",
                                        format = "png"
                                    })
                                    serverMap[token] = server.id
                                end
                            end
                            
                            serversChecked = serversChecked + 1
                            ScannerBtn.Text = seaName .. " | " .. serversChecked
                            
                            if #currentBatch >= 90 or _ == #sData.data then
                                local bSuccess, bResponse = pcall(function()
                                    return requestFunc({
                                        Url = "https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/batch",
                                        Method = "POST",
                                        Headers = {
                                            ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                                        },
                                        Body = HttpService:JSONEncode(currentBatch)
                                    })
                                end)
                                
                                if bSuccess and bResponse.StatusCode == 200 then
                                    local bData = HttpService:JSONDecode(bResponse.Body)
                                    if bData and bData.data then
                                        for _, thumb in pairs(bData.data) do
                                            local thumbHash = thumb.imageUrl and thumb.imageUrl:match("rbxcdn%.com/([%w%-]+)")
                                            if thumbHash and thumbHash == targetHash then
                                                local foundJobId = serverMap[thumb.requestId]
                                                isScanning = false
                                                ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)"
                                                ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                                                
                                                CreateConfirmationPrompt("Player Found in " .. seaName .. "!\nServer ID: " .. foundJobId, foundJobId, placeId, function()
                                                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, foundJobId, player)
                                                end, function()
                                                    SendNotification("Join cancelled.", 3)
                                                end)
                                                return
                                            end
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                                table.clear(currentBatch)
                                table.clear(serverMap)
                                task.wait()
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.01)
                    end
                end
                
                if isScanning then
                    SendNotification("Player not found.", 5)
                end
                
                isScanning = false
                ScannerBtn.Text = "JOIN PLAYER (JOINS OFF)"
                ScannerBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            end)
        end)
    end
