    -- === LOOPS ===

    -- HEARTBEAT LOOP (PHYSICS OVERRIDE)
    table.insert(Connections, RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
    end))
    
    
    -- STEPPED LOOP (NO CLIP LOGIC)
    table.insert(Connections, RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
        if Config.NoClip and character then
            for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.CanCollide then
                    part.CanCollide = false
                end
            end
        end
        
        if Config.AntiStun and character and humanoid and rootPart then
            humanoid.PlatformStand = false
            humanoid.Sit = false
            
            local speed = Config.WalkSpeedValue
            if speed < 16 then speed = 16 end -- Force minimum speed
            if humanoid.WalkSpeed < speed then humanoid.WalkSpeed = speed end
            
            if humanoid.JumpPower < Config.JumpPowerValue then humanoid.JumpPower = Config.JumpPowerValue end
            if rootPart.Anchored then rootPart.Anchored = false end -- Force Unanchor
            
            character:SetAttribute("Stun", 0)
            character:SetAttribute("Busy", false)
            character:SetAttribute("CantMove", false)
            character:SetAttribute("Stunned", false)
            
            -- Remove Stun BodyMovers
            for _, v in pairs(rootPart:GetChildren()) do
                if (v:IsA("BodyVelocity") or v:IsA("BodyGyro") or v:IsA("BodyPosition")) and v.Name ~= "FlyVelocity" and v.Name ~= "FlyGyro" and v.Name ~= "FarmVelocity" then
                    v:Destroy()
                end
            end
        end
        
        if Config.AntiChair and character and humanoid then
            local isSittingOnCreated = false
            if humanoid.SeatPart and humanoid.SeatPart.Name == "CreatedChair" then
                isSittingOnCreated = true
            end

            if not isSittingOnCreated then
                humanoid.Sit = false
                humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                -- Disable seated state completely
                humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
                -- Check if character is in a seat and force exit
                if character.Parent and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local seat = character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("SeatWeld")
                    if seat and seat.Part1 and seat.Part1.Name ~= "CreatedChair" then
                        seat:Destroy()
                    end
                    -- Check for vehicle seat
                    for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if (v:IsA("VehicleSeat") or v:IsA("Seat")) and v.Occupant == humanoid and v.Name ~= "CreatedChair" then
                            humanoid:Sit(nil)
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
            end
        else
            -- Re-enable seated state when AntiChair is disabled
            if humanoid then
                humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
            end
        end
        
        -- Infinite Energy Logic
        if Config.InfiniteEnergy and character and character:FindFirstChild("Energy") then
            pcall(function()
                character.Energy.Value = character.Energy.MaxValue
            end)
        end
    end))

    -- === FAST ATTACK / KILL AURA SYSTEM ===
    local function AttackFunction()
        local character = player.Character
        local tool = character and character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
        local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        
        if tool then
            -- Bypass attack animations
            if Config.NoCooldown and humanoid then
                pcall(function()
                    for _, track in pairs(humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()) do
                        if track.Name:lower():find("attack") or track.Name:lower():find("slash") or track.Name:lower():find("swing") then
                            track:Stop()
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end

            -- Spam M1 Remotes for Blox Fruits (Nuclear Fast Attack)
            task.spawn(function()
                pcall(function()
                    local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                    local remotes = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Remotes")
                    
                    if remotes and remotes:FindFirstChild("Validator") then
                        remotes.Validator:FireServer(math.floor(tick() * 1000))
                    end
                    
                    if tool:FindFirstChild("RemoteEvent") then
                        tool.RemoteEvent:FireServer("Attack")
                    end
                    
                    tool:Activate()
                end)
            end)
        end
    end

    -- DAMAGE FIX LOOP (Validator Spam for Ghost Hits)
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if (Config.Reach or Config.HitboxExpander) and UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1) then
                pcall(function()
                    local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                    if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("Remotes") and ReplicatedStorage.Remotes:FindFirstChild("Validator") then
                        ReplicatedStorage.Remotes.Validator:FireServer(math.floor(tick() * 1000))
                    end
                end)
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end)

    local function EquipSelectedWeapon()
        if not player.Character or not player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then return end
        local humanoid = player.Character.Humanoid
        local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
        
        if Config.SelectedWeapon then
            local toolInHand = player.Character:FindFirstChild(Config.SelectedWeapon)
            if not toolInHand and backpack then
                local tool = backpack:FindFirstChild(Config.SelectedWeapon)
                if tool then
                    humanoid:EquipTool(tool)
                end
            end
        end
    end

    -- DEDICATED KILL AURA LOOP (NUCLEAR SPAM)
    local lastCooldownScan = 0
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            -- 1. No Cooldown Logic (Aggressive & Optimized)
            if Config.NoCooldown then
                local currentTime = tick()
                
                -- Scan every 0.1 seconds for better responsiveness
                if currentTime - lastCooldownScan > 0.1 then
                    lastCooldownScan = currentTime
                    
                    local character = player.Character
                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                    
                    local function wipeCooldowns(container)
                        if not container then return end
                        for _, v in pairs(container:GetDescendants()) do
                            if v:IsA("ValueBase") then
                                local vName = v.Name:lower()
                                if vName:find("cooldown") or vName:find("cd") or vName:find("skill") or vName:find("timer") or vName:find("ability") or vName:find("stun") or vName:find("busy") or vName:find("using") then
                                    pcall(function() 
                                        if v:IsA("StringValue") then v.Value = "" 
                                        elseif v:IsA("BoolValue") then v.Value = false
                                        else v.Value = 0 end 
                                    end)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end

                    wipeCooldowns(character)
                    wipeCooldowns(backpack)
                    
                    -- Handle Attributes more aggressively
                    if character then
                        for _, attr in pairs({"Stun", "Busy", "Cooldown", "AbilityCooldown", "SkillCooldown", "LastUse", "NextUse", "Using", "Casting", "Attacking"}) do
                            pcall(function() character:SetAttribute(attr, 0) end)
                            pcall(function() character:SetAttribute(attr, false) end)
                        end
                    end
                    
                    if backpack then
                        for _, tool in pairs(backpack:GetChildren()) do
                            if tool:IsA("Tool") then
                                for _, attr in pairs({"Cooldown", "SkillCooldown", "AbilityCooldown", "LastUse", "NextUse"}) do
                                    pcall(function() tool:SetAttribute(attr, 0) end)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    
                    -- UI Cooldown Hiding
                    pcall(function()
                        local playerGui = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui")
                        if playerGui then
                            for _, v in pairs(playerGui:GetDescendants()) do
                                if (v:IsA("Frame") or v:IsA("ImageLabel") or v:IsA("TextLabel")) then
                                    local vName = v.Name:lower()
                                    if vName:find("cooldown") or vName:find("cd") or vName:find("timer") then
                                        -- Skip cheat GUI
                                        if not (vName:find("cyber") or vName:find("desync") or vName:find("esp")) then
                                            v.Visible = false
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end

            -- 2. Force Attack & Skill Spam (Aggressive Nuclear Mode)
            if Config.NoCooldown and player.Character then
                local tool = player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                if tool then
                    -- Force activate and fire attack events
                    pcall(function()
                        tool:Activate()
                        if tool:FindFirstChild("RemoteEvent") then
                            for i = 1, 3 do
                                tool.RemoteEvent:FireServer("Attack")
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    -- Spam common skill remotes (Blox Fruits / RPG styles)
                    pcall(function()
                        local remotes = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Remotes") or game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                        local commF = remotes:FindFirstChild("CommF_")
                        
                        if commF then
                            local skills = {"Z", "X", "C", "V", "F"}
                            for _, key in ipairs(skills) do
                                task.spawn(function()
                                    commF:InvokeServer("Skill", key, true)
                                    commF:InvokeServer("Skill", key, false)
                                end)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end

            -- 3. Kill Aura Logic
            if Config.KillAura and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local myRoot = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                -- Auto Equip Weapon
                EquipSelectedWeapon()
                if not player.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") and player:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
                    local toolToEquip = nil
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
                        if t:IsA("Tool") then
                            local n = t.Name:lower()
                            if n:find("sword") or n:find("blade") or n:find("katana") or n:find("saber") or n:find("cutlass") or n:find("cdk") or n:find("yru") or n:find("trident") or n:find("melee") or n:find("combat") then
                                toolToEquip = t
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if not toolToEquip then toolToEquip = player.Backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") end
                    if toolToEquip and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then player.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(toolToEquip) end
                end

                local target = nil
                local minDist = Config.AuraRange
                
                -- Target Selection
                if Config.EasyLock and Config.TargetName ~= "None" then
                    local lockedPlr = Players:FindFirstChild(Config.TargetName)
                    if lockedPlr and lockedPlr.Character and lockedPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and lockedPlr.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        target = lockedPlr.Character
                    end
                end

                if not target then
                    -- Scan Players
                    for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            local isEnemy = true
                            if Config.TeamCheck and p.Team and player.Team and p.Team == player.Team then isEnemy = false end
                            
                            if isEnemy then
                                local dist = (myRoot.Position - p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                if dist < minDist then
                                    minDist = dist
                                    target = p.Character
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    -- Scan NPCs
                    local function scan(folder)
                        if not folder then return end
                        for _, v in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
                            if v:IsA("Model") and v ~= player.Character and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                if not Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(v) then
                                    local dist = (myRoot.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                    if dist < minDist then
                                        minDist = dist
                                        target = v
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    scan(workspace)
                    scan(workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies"))
                end

                -- Attack Execution
                if target and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local targetRoot = target.HumanoidRootPart
                    -- Aggressive Fast Attack (Spam M1)
                    for i = 1, 15 do
                        AttackFunction()
                    end
                    
                    -- Hitbox Extender for Aura
                    if firetouchinterest then
                        firetouchinterest(myRoot, targetRoot, 0)
                        firetouchinterest(myRoot, targetRoot, 1)
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.01) -- High Frequency
        end
    end)
    
    -- ANTI LAVA / DAMAGE BLOCK LOGIC
    task.spawn(function()
        local wasEnabled = false
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.AntiLava then
                if not wasEnabled then
                    wasEnabled = true
                    -- FFlag Method (User Request)
                    pcall(function()
                        if setfflag then
                            setfflag("DFIntTouchSenderMaxBandwidthBpsScaling", "-1")
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    -- Scan specific zones (Optimized to prevent freeze)
                    task.spawn(function()
                        local zones = {
                            Vector3.new(-5191.37, 177.50, -5503.91),
                            Vector3.new(913.16, 249.09, 32869.20)
                        }
                        local radius = 4000 -- Large radius to cover islands/dungeons

                        for _, center in ipairs(zones) do
                            if not Config.AntiLava then break end
                            local parts = workspace:GetPartBoundsInRadius(center, radius)
                            for i, part in ipairs(parts) do
                                if not Config.AntiLava then break end
                                disableDamageBlock(part)
                                if i % 500 == 0 then task.wait() end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    
                    -- Listen for new parts (StreamingEnabled / Raids)
                    if not antiLavaConnection then
                        antiLavaConnection = Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(disableDamageBlock)
                    end
                end
            else
                if wasEnabled then
                    wasEnabled = false
                    if antiLavaConnection then
                        antiLavaConnection:Disconnect()
                        antiLavaConnection = nil
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait(1)
        end
    end)
    
    -- WALK ON WATER LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        local platform = Instance.new("Part")
        platform.Name = "WaterPlatform"
        platform.Size = Vector3.new(20, 1, 20)
        platform.Transparency = 1 -- Invisible

                platform.Parent = nil
            end
            task.wait(0.05)
        end
        if platform then platform:Destroy() end
    end)

    -- TRIGGER BOT LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.TriggerBot then
                local shouldShoot = false
                local targetScreenPos = nil
                
                -- 1. CHECK SILENT AIM TARGET (IN FOV)
                if Config.SilentAim then
                    local target = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                    if target and target.Character then
                        local targetPart = target.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if targetPart then
                            local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(targetPart.Position)
                            if onScreen then
                                shouldShoot = true
                                targetScreenPos = Vector2.new(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                elseif not shouldShoot then
                    -- 2. CHECK MOUSE TARGET (FALLBACK)
                    local target = mouse.Target
                    if target and target.Parent then
                        local model = target.Parent
                        if model ~= character then
                            local hum = model:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if hum and hum.Health > 0 then
                                local root = model:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or model:FindFirstChild("Head")
                                if root then
                                    local dist = (root.Position - camera.CFrame.Position).Magnitude
                                    if dist <= Config.TriggerDistance then
                                        shouldShoot = true
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                -- 4. FIRE
                if shouldShoot then
                    NuclearClick(targetScreenPos)
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end)
    
    -- REMOVE FOG LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.RemoveFog then
                Lighting.FogEnd = 9e9
                Lighting.FogStart = 9e9
                for _, v in pairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
                    if v:IsA("Atmosphere") then v:Destroy() end
                end
            end
            task.wait(1)
        end
    end)
    
    -- AUTO RAID LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        local wasAutoRaid = false
        local LastRaidTargetTime = 0
        
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.AutoRaid then
                wasAutoRaid = true
                
                -- Enable Anti Lava
                if not Config.AntiLava then
                    Config.AntiLava = true
                    if ToggleButtons["AntiLava"] then ToggleButtons["AntiLava"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor end
                end
                
                pcall(function()
                    if character and rootPart and humanoid then
                        local closest = nil
                        local minDist = math.huge
                        local scanRange = 5000 -- Increased Range
                        
                        if workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies") then
                            for _, v in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                if v:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    local dist = (rootPart.Position - v.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                    if dist < minDist and dist < scanRange then
                                        minDist = dist
                                        closest = v
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        if closest then
                            LastRaidTargetTime = os.clock()
                            local targetHRP = closest.HumanoidRootPart
                            
                            -- TP
                            rootPart.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)
                            
                            -- Hitbox
                            rootPart.Size = Vector3.new(25, 25, 25)
                            rootPart.Transparency = 1
                            rootPart.CanCollide = false
                            
                            -- Equip
                            EquipSelectedWeapon()
                            local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                            if not tool then
                                local bp = player.Backpack
                                if bp then
                                    local t = bp:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                                    if t then humanoid:EquipTool(t) end
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Click
                            if tool then tool:Activate() end
                            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(camera.ViewportSize.X/2, camera.ViewportSize.Y/2, 0, true, game, 1)
                            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseButtonEvent(camera.ViewportSize.X/2, camera.ViewportSize.Y/2, 0, false, game, 1)
                            
                            rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                            rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                        else
                            -- No target found: Move Forward
                            if os.clock() - LastRaidTargetTime > 5 then
                                humanoid.PlatformStand = true
                                rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                                rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                                
                                -- Move forward relative to character facing
                                rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -5)
                                
                                for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                if wasAutoRaid then
                    wasAutoRaid = false
                    LastRaidTargetTime = os.clock()
                    
                    -- Reset Character
                    if character and rootPart then
                        rootPart.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
                        rootPart.Transparency = 1
                        rootPart.CanCollide = true
                        if humanoid then
                            humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    LastRaidTargetTime = os.clock()
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end)
    
    -- SEA EVENT LOGIC (Leviathan & Boat)
    task.spawn(function()
        local TikiOutpostPos = Vector3.new(-16913.67, 9.40, 510.33)
        local Zone6Position = Vector3.new(-40000, 10, -5000)
        
        local function TweenTo(targetPos)
            if character and rootPart and rootPart.Parent then
                local dist = (rootPart.Position - targetPos).Magnitude
                if dist < 50 then return end
                
                local speed = 350
                local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local tween = TweenService:Create(rootPart, info, {CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)})
                
                local conn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                    if character then
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                tween:Play()
                
                -- Wait for completion or cancellation
                while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                    if not Config.IsRunning or (not Config.AutoFindLeviathan and not Config.AutoBuyBoat) then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    if not character or not rootPart or not rootPart.Parent or (humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0) then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
                
                if conn then conn:Disconnect() end
            end
        end
        
        local function BuyAndSit()
            if not rootPart or not humanoid then return end
            -- 1. Go to Tiki
            if (rootPart.Position - TikiOutpostPos).Magnitude > 500 then
                TweenTo(TikiOutpostPos)
            end
            rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(TikiOutpostPos)
            task.wait(0.5)
            
            -- 2. Buy
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", Config.SelectedBoat)
            task.wait(1.5)
            
            -- 3. Sit
            local seatFound = nil
            local searchList = workspace:GetChildren()
            if workspace:FindFirstChild("Boats") then searchList = workspace.Boats:GetChildren() end
            
            for _, v in pairs(searchList) do
                if (v.Name:find("Boat") or v.Name == Config.SelectedBoat) then
                    local seat = v:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") or v:FindFirstChild("DriverSeat") or v:FindFirstChild("Seat")
                    if seat and (seat.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude < 200 then
                        seatFound = seat
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if seatFound and rootPart and humanoid then
                rootPart.CFrame = seatFound.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                task.wait(0.2)
                seatFound:Sit(humanoid)
            end
        end

        while Config.IsRunning do
            pcall(function()
                -- AUTO BUY BOAT ONLY
                if Config.AutoBuyBoat then
                    if character and rootPart and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        if not humanoid.SeatPart then
                            BuyAndSit()
                        end
                    end
                    Config.AutoBuyBoat = false
                    if ToggleButtons["AutoBuyBoat"] then ToggleButtons["AutoBuyBoat"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) end
                end
                
                -- AUTO FIND LEVIATHAN (FULL SEQUENCE)
                if Config.AutoFindLeviathan then
                    if character and rootPart and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                        -- 1. Buy/Sit if not seated
                        if not humanoid.SeatPart then
                            BuyAndSit()
                        end
                        
                        -- 2. Drive to Zone 6
                        if humanoid.SeatPart then
                            local vehicle = humanoid.SeatPart.Parent
                            local primary = vehicle.PrimaryPart or humanoid.SeatPart
                            
                            local dist = (primary.Position - Zone6Position).Magnitude
                            if dist > 500 then
                                local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / 350, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                                local tween = TweenService:Create(primary, info, {CFrame = CFrame.new(Zone6Position)})
                                
                                local noclipConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                                    for _, v in pairs(vehicle:GetDescendants()) do
                                        if v:IsA("BasePart") then 
                                            v.CanCollide = false 
                                            v.Transparency = 0.5
                                        end
                                    end
                                end)
                                
                                tween:Play()
                                
                                while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                                    if not Config.AutoFindLeviathan then tween:Cancel() break end
                                    if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Frozen Watcher") then tween:Cancel() break end
                                    if not humanoid.SeatPart then tween:Cancel() break end
                                    task.wait(0.1)
                                end
                                
                                if noclipConn then noclipConn:Disconnect() end
                                primary.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- 3. Wait/Go to Frozen Watcher
                        local watcher = workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Frozen Watcher")
                        if watcher and watcher:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            TweenTo(watcher.HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 30, 0))
                        end
                        
                        -- 4. Spam Gate
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("FrozenDimension")
                    end
                end
            end)
            task.wait(1)
        end
    end)
    
    -- MASTERY FARM LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        local points = {
            Vector3.new(45.54, 99.37, -12605.42),
            Vector3.new(111.02, 100.24, -12933.88),
            Vector3.new(724, 94.46, -12617.58),
            Vector3.new(-13.85, 94.62, -12262.23)
        }
        
        local function TweenTo(targetPos)
            if character and rootPart and rootPart.Parent then
                local dist = (rootPart.Position - targetPos).Magnitude
                if dist < 5 then return end
                
                local speed = 300 
                local info = TweenInfo.new(dist / speed, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
                local tween = TweenService:Create(rootPart, info, {CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos)})
                
                local noclipConn = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                    if character then
                        for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                            if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                tween:Play()
                
                while tween.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
                    if not Config.IsRunning or not Config.MasteryFarm then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    if not character or not rootPart or not rootPart.Parent or (humanoid and humanoid.Health <= 0) then
                        tween:Cancel()
                        break
                    end
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
                
                if noclipConn then noclipConn:Disconnect() end
                if rootPart then rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) end
            end
        end

        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.MasteryFarm then
                EquipSelectedWeapon()
                for _, point in ipairs(points) do
                    if not Config.MasteryFarm then break end
                    
                    TweenTo(point)
                    
                    if Config.MasteryFarm then
                        local startWait = tick()
                        while tick() - startWait < 4 do
                            if not Config.MasteryFarm then break end
                            if rootPart then 
                                rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) 
                                rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(point)
                            end
                            task.wait(0.1)
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end)

    -- FAKE LAG LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.FakeLag and character and rootPart then
                rootPart.Anchored = true
                task.wait(0.2)
                if rootPart then rootPart.Anchored = false end
                task.wait()
            else
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- DESYNC LOGIC - Clone immobile visible aux autres
    local desyncClone = nil
    local isDesyncEnabled = false
    
    local function enableDesync()
        if not character or not rootPart then return end
        isDesyncEnabled = true
        
        -- CrÃ©er un clone du character
        if not desyncClone then
            desyncClone = character:Clone()
            desyncClone.Name = character.Name
            desyncClone.Parent = Workspace
            
            -- DÃ©sactiver les scripts du clone
            for _, script in pairs(desyncClone:GetDescendants()) do
                if script:IsA("LocalScript") or script:IsA("Script") then
                    script:Destroy()
                end
            end
            
            -- DÃ©sactiver l'humanoid du clone (il ne peut pas mourir)
            local cloneHum = desyncClone:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            if cloneHum then
                cloneHum.MaxHealth = math.huge
                cloneHum.Health = math.huge
            end
            
            -- Geler le clone Ã  la position actuelle
            if desyncClone:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local cloneRoot = desyncClone.HumanoidRootPart
                cloneRoot.Anchored = true
                cloneRoot.CanCollide = false
                cloneRoot.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame
            end
        end
        
        -- Geler le vrai character avec Anchored (ne bouge pas cÃ´tÃ© serveur)
        rootPart.Anchored = true
        
        -- Rendre le vrai character invisible
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.Transparency = 1
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
    end
    
    local function disableDesync()
        if not character then return end
        isDesyncEnabled = false
        
        -- DÃ©truire le clone
        if desyncClone then
            desyncClone:Destroy()
            desyncClone = nil
        end
        
        -- DÃ©geler le vrai character
        if rootPart then
            rootPart.Anchored = false
            rootPart.CanCollide = true
        end
        
        -- Rendre le vrai character visible Ã  nouveau
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.Transparency = 0
                part.CanCollide = true
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- DESYNC LOOP - Bouger le vrai character invisible
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if isDesyncEnabled and character and rootPart then
                -- Mouvement normal du character (invisible)
                if humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    -- Appliquer la vitesse de marche normalement
                    if Config.WalkSpeedValue > 0 then
                        humanoid.WalkSpeed = Config.WalkSpeedValue
                    end
                end
                
                task.wait(0.016)
            else
                task.wait(0.1)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- FARM NEAREST LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.FarmNearest and character and rootPart then
                -- Auto Equip Sword
                EquipSelectedWeapon()
                if character and not character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") and player:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
                    local toolToEquip = nil
                    for _, t in pairs(player.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
                        if t:IsA("Tool") then
                            if t.Name:lower():find("sword") or t.Name:lower():find("blade") or t.Name:lower():find("katana") or t.Name:lower():find("saber") or t.Name:lower():find("cutlass") then
                                toolToEquip = t
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if not toolToEquip then toolToEquip = player.Backpack:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool") end
                    if toolToEquip and humanoid then humanoid:EquipTool(toolToEquip) end
                end
                
                local target = nil
                local minDist = 99999
                
                -- Helper to scan folders
                local function scanFolder(folder)
                    for _, obj in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
                        if obj:IsA("Model") and obj ~= character and obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if obj.Humanoid.Health > 0 and not Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(obj) then
                                local dist = (rootPart.Position - obj.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                                if dist < minDist then
                                    minDist = dist
                                    target = obj
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                scanFolder(Workspace)
                if Workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies") then scanFolder(Workspace.Enemies) end
                
                local function bringMobs(folder)
                    for _, obj in pairs(folder:GetChildren()) do
                        if obj:IsA("Model") and obj ~= character and obj:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and obj:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                            if obj.Humanoid.Health > 0 and not Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(obj) then
                                local eRoot = obj.HumanoidRootPart
                                if (eRoot.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude <= Config.BringRange then
                                    eRoot.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -15, 0) -- Bring under player
                                    eRoot.CanCollide = false
                                    eRoot.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                                    eRoot.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                if target then
                    local tHum = target.Humanoid
                    local tRoot = target.HumanoidRootPart
                    
                    -- Enable Fly (BodyVelocity)
                    local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FarmVelocity")
                    if not bv then
                        bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                        bv.Name = "FarmVelocity"
                        bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
                        bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                        bv.Parent = rootPart
                    end
                    
                    -- Attack Loop
                    while Config.FarmNearest and target and tHum.Health > 0 and rootPart do
                        -- Fly Logic (Tween/Lerp to target)
                        local targetPos = tRoot.Position + Vector3.new(0, 20, 0) -- 20 studs above
                        rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame:Lerp(CFrame.new(targetPos, tRoot.Position), 0.5)
                        
                        -- Bring Mobs
                        if Config.BringMob then
                            bringMobs(Workspace)
                            if Workspace:FindFirstChild("Enemies") then bringMobs(Workspace.Enemies) end
                        end
                        
                        -- Spam Click
                        local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(tRoot.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            NuclearClick(Vector2.new(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y))
                        else
                            NuclearClick()
                        end
                        
                        RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
                    end
                else
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            else
                if rootPart then
                    local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FarmVelocity")
                    if bv then bv:Destroy() end
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end)
    
    -- ORBIT PLAYER LOOP
    local orbitRot = 10
    table.insert(Connections, RunService.Stepped:Connect(function(t, dt)
        if Config.OrbitPlayer and Config.OrbitPlayerTarget ~= "" and character and rootPart then
            local targetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(Config.OrbitPlayerTarget)
            if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
                local targetRoot = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if targetRoot then
                    local speed = 1
                    local radius = 1 -- Increased from 2 to 5 for better visibility
                    local eclipse = 1
                    local rotation = CFrame.Angles(100, 50, 0)
                    
                    local sin, cos = math.sin, math.cos
                    local rotspeed = math.pi * 2 / speed
                    eclipse = eclipse * radius
                    
                    orbitRot = orbitRot + dt * rotspeed
                    rootPart.CFrame = rotation * CFrame.new(sin(orbitRot) * eclipse, 0, cos(orbitRot) * radius) + targetRoot.Position
                    
                    rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                    rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
                end
            end
        end
    end))

    -- PANIC MODE LOOP
    table.insert(Connections, RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        -- Auto Panic Logic
        if Config.PanicModeHealthEnable and character and humanoid then
            if humanoid.Health > 0 then
                if not Config.PanicMode and humanoid.Health <= Config.PanicModeMinHealth then
                    Config.PanicMode = true
                    if ToggleButtons["PanicMode"] then
                        ToggleButtons["PanicMode"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    end
                elseif Config.PanicMode and humanoid.Health >= Config.PanicModeMaxHealth then
                    Config.PanicMode = false
                    if ToggleButtons["PanicMode"] then
                        ToggleButtons["PanicMode"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if Config.PanicMode and character and rootPart then
            if humanoid then
                humanoid.PlatformStand = true
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics)
            end
            
            -- Move up very fast (Infinite Ascent)
            rootPart.CFrame = rootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10000, 0)
            rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 100000, 0)
            
            -- Force Noclip
            for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if v:IsA("BasePart") then v.CanCollide = false end
            end
        end
    end))

    -- === AIM ASSIST / FLICK ON ATTACK (FIX FOR SKILLS) ===
    RunService:BindToRenderStep("AimLockPriority", Enum.RenderPriority.Camera.Value + 1, function()
        if Config.SilentAim then
            if IsCombatKeyDown() then
                -- Verrouillage "Sticky" : on garde la mÃªme cible tant qu'on appuie
                if not combatTarget then
                    combatTarget = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
                end
                
                if combatTarget and combatTarget.Character and combatTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and combatTarget.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    -- PrioritÃ© au Torse (HumanoidRootPart) car plus gros
                    local targetPart = combatTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or combatTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or combatTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if targetPart then
                        local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(targetPart.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            VirtualInputManager:SendMouseMoveEvent(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y, game)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    combatTarget = nil -- Cible perdue ou morte
                end
            else
                combatTarget = nil -- Touche relÃ¢chÃ©e
            end
        end
        
        -- CURSOR LOCK LOGIC
        if Config.CursorLock then
            -- 1. Persistent User Check
            if Config.CursorLockUser ~= "" then
                local targetPlr = nil
                for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if p ~= player and (p.Name:lower():find(Config.CursorLockUser:lower()) or p.DisplayName:lower():find(Config.CursorLockUser:lower())) then
                        targetPlr = p
                        break
                    end
                end
                
                if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and targetPlr.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                     cursorLockTarget = targetPlr.Character
                     CursorLabel.Text = "PERSISTENT: " .. targetPlr.Name
                     CursorLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                end
            end

            if cursorLockTarget then
                 if cursorLockTarget.Parent and cursorLockTarget:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and cursorLockTarget.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    local targetPart = cursorLockTarget:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or cursorLockTarget:FindFirstChild("Torso") or cursorLockTarget:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or cursorLockTarget:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if targetPart then
                        local screenPos, onScreen = camera:WorldToViewportPoint(targetPart.Position)
                        if onScreen then
                            pcall(function() VirtualInputManager:SendMouseMoveEvent(screenPos.X, screenPos.Y, game) end)
                        end
                    end
                 else
                    if Config.CursorLockUser == "" then
                        cursorLockTarget = nil
                        CursorLabel.Text = "Status: Target Lost"
                        CursorLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                    end
                 end
            end
        end
        
        -- AIMLOCK LOGIC (Moved to BindToRenderStep for Priority)
        if Config.Aimlock or Config.ZoneLock then
            -- 2. Zone Trigger (Distance)
            if Config.ZoneLock and (not aimlockTarget or aimlockEndTime ~= math.huge) then
                if not aimlockTarget and rootPart and tick() > aimlockCooldown then
                    local minDist = Config.ZoneDistance
                    local targetFound = nil
                    
                    for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if p ~= player and p.Character and p.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and p.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            local dist = (rootPart.Position - p.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                            if dist < minDist then
                                minDist = dist
                                targetFound = p.Character
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    
                    if targetFound then
                        aimlockTarget = targetFound
                        aimlockEndTime = tick() + Config.ZoneDuration
                    end
                end
            end
            
            -- Check Expiry (Global)
            if aimlockTarget and tick() > aimlockEndTime then
                aimlockTarget = nil
                aimlockCooldown = tick() + Config.ZoneCooldown
            end
            
            -- 2. Apply Lock
            if aimlockTarget then
                if aimlockTarget.Parent and aimlockTarget:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and aimlockTarget.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    local root = aimlockTarget:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or aimlockTarget:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if root then
                        camera.CFrame = CFrame.new(camera.CFrame.Position, root.Position)
                    else
                        aimlockTarget = nil
                    end
                else
                    aimlockTarget = nil
                end
            end
        end

        -- MOUSE CLICK LOCK LOGIC
        if Config.MouseClickLock then
            if UserInputService:IsMouseButtonPressed(Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton2) then
                if not mouseClickTarget then
                    mouseClickTarget = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.MouseClickFOV > 0 and Config.MouseClickFOV or 100, true)
                end
                
                if mouseClickTarget and mouseClickTarget.Character and mouseClickTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and mouseClickTarget.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                    local root = mouseClickTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or mouseClickTarget.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if root then
                        camera.CFrame = CFrame.new(camera.CFrame.Position, root.Position)
                    end
                else
                    mouseClickTarget = nil
                end
            else
                mouseClickTarget = nil
            end
        end
    end)

    table.insert(Connections, workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(descendant)
        if Config.ToolColorChanger then
            applyToolColor(descendant)
        end
    end))

    table.insert(Connections, RunService.Stepped:Connect(function(_, deltaTime)
    end))
    
    table.insert(Connections, RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(deltaTime)
        UpdateESP()

        -- TOOL COLOR CHANGER LOGIC (EXPANDED)
        if Config.ToolColorChanger and character then
            for _, descendant in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                applyToolColor(descendant)
            end
        end
        
        -- Trigger FlashStep Logic (Spam R while hovering)
        if Config.TriggerFlashStep and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
            local target = mouse.Target
            local targetPlayer = nil
            if target and target.Parent and target.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                targetPlayer = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(target.Parent)
            end

            if targetPlayer and targetPlayer ~= player and (Config.TriggerFlashStepUser == "" or targetPlayer.Name == Config.TriggerFlashStepUser) then
                -- Spam R key while hovering over enemy
                task.spawn(function()
                    VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.R, false, game)
                    task.wait(0.05)
                    VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(false, Enum.KeyCode.R, false, game)
                end)
            end
        end
        
        -- FOV CHANGER
        if camera and Config.FOVValue ~= 70 then
            camera.FieldOfView = Config.FOVValue
        end
        
        -- HITBOX EXTENDER LOGIC
        if Config.HitboxExpander then
            wasHitboxExpanded = true
            for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if p ~= player and p.Character then
                    local shouldExpand = false
                    if Config.HitboxModeAll then
                        shouldExpand = true
                    else
                        if Config.HitboxTargetUser ~= "" and string.find(p.Name:lower(), Config.HitboxTargetUser:lower()) then
                            shouldExpand = true
                        end
                    end

                    if shouldExpand then
                        for _, part in pairs(p.Character:GetChildren()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and (part.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" or part.Name == "Head" or part.Name == "Torso" or part.Name == "UpperTorso" or part.Name == "LowerTorso") then
                                if not part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                                    part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", part.Size)
                                end
                                part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.HitboxSize
                                part.Transparency = Config.HitboxTransparency
                                part.CanCollide = false
                                part.CanTouch = true -- Assure que les Ã©vÃ©nements Touched fonctionnent
                                pcall(function() part.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball end) -- Force Round Hitbox
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        -- Reset non-targets if they were expanded
                        local hum = p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                        for _, part in pairs(p.Character:GetChildren()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                                part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize")
                                part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", nil)
                                if part.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
                                    part.Transparency = 1
                                    part.CanCollide = true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                            task.spawn(function()
                                pcall(function()
                                    local desc = Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(p.UserId)
                                    if desc then ApplyDescriptionCustom(hum, desc) end
                                end)
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                end
        elseif wasHitboxExpanded then
            wasHitboxExpanded = false
            for _, p in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if p ~= player and p.Character then
                    local hum = p.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                    for _, part in pairs(p.Character:GetChildren()) do
                        if part:IsA("BasePart") and part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                            part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize")
                            part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", nil)
                            if part.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
                                part.Transparency = 1
                                part.CanCollide = true
                            end
                        end
                    end
                        task.spawn(function()
                            pcall(function()
                                local desc = Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(p.UserId)
                                if desc then ApplyDescriptionCustom(hum, desc) end
                            end)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        
        -- PART EXTENDER LOGIC (Extend specific body parts of self)
        if Config.PartExtender and character then
            local partMap = {
                Head = Config.PartExtenderHead,
                Torso = Config.PartExtenderTorso,
                UpperTorso = Config.PartExtenderTorso,
                LowerTorso = Config.PartExtenderTorso,
                ["Left Arm"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftArm,
                ["LeftUpperArm"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftArm,
                ["LeftLowerArm"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftArm,
                ["Right Arm"] = Config.PartExtenderRightArm,
                ["RightUpperArm"] = Config.PartExtenderRightArm,
                ["RightLowerArm"] = Config.PartExtenderRightArm,
                ["Left Leg"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftLeg,
                ["LeftUpperLeg"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftLeg,
                ["LeftLowerLeg"] = Config.PartExtenderLeftLeg,
                ["Right Leg"] = Config.PartExtenderRightLeg,
                ["RightUpperLeg"] = Config.PartExtenderRightLeg,
                ["RightLowerLeg"] = Config.PartExtenderRightLeg
            }
            
            for _, part in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") and partMap[part.Name] then
                    if not part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                        part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", part.Size)
                    end
                    part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.PartExtenderSize
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- SELF REACH LOGIC (Avatar & Tool Extender)
        if Config.Reach and character then
            -- Global Reach (Tout le corps + Accessoires + Outils)
            -- Global Reach (Optimized for Sanguine Art & Melee)
            for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
                    if not part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                        part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", part.Size)
                    end
                    part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.ReachSize
                    part.CanCollide = false
                    part.Massless = true
                    part.Transparency = Config.ReachTransparency
                    part.CanTouch = true
                    part.CanQuery = true
                    part.CanQuery = false
                    pcall(function() part.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball end) -- Force Round Hitbox
                end
            end
            
            -- Listener for transient hitboxes (M1s / Skills)
            if not reachConnection then
                reachConnection = character.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(child)
                    if Config.Reach and child:IsA("BasePart") and child.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
                        if not child:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then child:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", child.Size) end
                        child.Size = child:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.ReachSize
                        child.CanCollide = false
                        child.Massless = true
                        child.Transparency = Config.ReachTransparency
                        child.CanTouch = true
                        child.CanQuery = true
                        child.CanQuery = false
                        pcall(function() child.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball end)
                    end
                end)
            end
        else
            if reachConnection then
                reachConnection:Disconnect()
                reachConnection = nil
                -- Restore Sizes
                if character then
                    for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                        if part:IsA("BasePart") and part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                            part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize")
                            part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", nil)
                        end
                    end
                end
                -- Reset Character Appearance
                task.spawn(function()
                    pcall(function()
                        local desc = Players:GetHumanoidDescriptionFromUserId(player.UserId)
                        if desc and humanoid then ApplyDescriptionCustom(humanoid, desc) end
                    end)
                end)
            end
        end
        
        -- UPDATE FOV CIRCLE (VISUALS)
        if Config.SilentAim and Config.ShowFOV then
            FOVCircle.Visible = true
            FOVCircle.Radius = Config.SilentFOV
            FOVCircle.Position = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()
            
            -- Visual feedback if target is in range
            local target = getClosestPlayerToMouse(Config.SilentFOV, true)
            if target then
                FOVCircle.Color = CurrentThemeColor -- Theme Color (Target Found)
            else
                FOVCircle.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) -- White (Unlocked)
            end
        else
            FOVCircle.Visible = false
        end
        
        -- STANDARD FLY (FIXED: NO ANCHOR, USE BODYVELOCITY)
        if Config.StandardFly and character and rootPart and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
            local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyVelocity")
            if not bv then
                bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                bv.Name = "FlyVelocity"
                bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
                bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                bv.Parent = rootPart
            end
            
            local bg = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyGyro")
            if not bg then
                bg = Instance.new("BodyGyro")
                bg.Name = "FlyGyro"
                bg.P = 9e4
                bg.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
                bg.cframe = rootPart.CFrame
                bg.Parent = rootPart
            end

            local camCF = camera.CFrame
            local moveDir = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.W) then moveDir = moveDir + camCF.LookVector end
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.S) then moveDir = moveDir - camCF.LookVector end
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.A) then moveDir = moveDir - camCF.RightVector end
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.D) then moveDir = moveDir + camCF.RightVector end
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space) then moveDir = moveDir + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
            if UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl) then moveDir = moveDir - Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end
            
            bg.CFrame = camCF
            
            -- Allow jump while flying (don't override PlatformStand when Space is pressed)
            local isJumping = UserInputService:IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode.Space)
            
            -- Only apply PlatformStand if not jumping (allows jumping while flying)
            -- Use Physics state instead of RunningNoPhysics to allow jump inputs to work
            if humanoid and not isJumping then
                humanoid.PlatformStand = true
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics)
            elseif humanoid and isJumping then
                -- Allow normal jump behavior
                humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
            end
            
            -- Disable seated state (getting up from chair)
            if humanoid.Sit then
                humanoid.Sit = false
            end
            
            -- Always update velocity based on current FlySpeedValue (even when not moving)
            -- This ensures speed changes take effect immediately
            if moveDir.Magnitude > 0 then
                bv.Velocity = moveDir.Unit * (Config.FlySpeedValue * 4)
            else
                bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
            end
        else
            -- Cleanup
            if rootPart then
                local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyVelocity")
                if bv then bv:Destroy() end
                local bg = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyGyro")
                if bg then bg:Destroy() end
            end
            -- Reset humanoid states to allow jumping and getting up from chairs
            if humanoid then
                humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                humanoid.Sit = false
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
            end
        end
        
        if Config.SpeedHack and humanoid then
            humanoid.WalkSpeed = Config.WalkSpeedValue
        end
        
        if Config.EasyLock and Config.TargetName ~= "None" and character and rootPart then
            local targetPlr = Players:FindFirstChild(Config.TargetName)
            if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character and targetPlr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local targetRoot = targetPlr.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                
                -- Improved "Untouchable" Strafing Logic (God Mode Movement)
                local t = tick()
                local baseRadius = Config.FollowDistance
                if baseRadius < 10 then baseRadius = 20 end -- Increased radius for better dodging
                
                -- Optimized movement to reduce Ping/Lag
                local radius = baseRadius + math.sin(t * 2) * 4 
                local angle = t * 4.5 
                local height = math.sin(t * 2.5) * 4 
                -- Optimized movement to reduce Ping/Lag & Anti-Kick
                local radius = baseRadius -- Fixed radius to prevent rubberbanding
                local angle = t * 2.2 -- Slower rotation to avoid speed checks
                local height = math.sin(t * 1.5) * 3 -- Smoother vertical oscillation
                
                local offset = Vector3.new(math.cos(angle) * radius, height, math.sin(angle) * radius)
                local newPos = targetRoot.Position + offset
                
                rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(newPos, targetRoot.Position)
                
                rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                rootPart.AssemblyAngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                rootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0) -- Legacy velocity reset
                local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyVelocity")
                if not bv then
                    bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
                    bv.Name = "FlyVelocity"
                    bv.Velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
                    bv.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
                    bv.Parent = rootPart
                end
            else
                Config.EasyLock = false
                if ToggleButtons["EasyLock"] then ToggleButtons["EasyLock"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) end
                Config.TargetName = "None"
                TargetLabel.Text = "Status: Target Lost"
                TargetLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyVelocity")
                if bv then bv:Destroy() end
            end
        end
        
        -- AUTO RACE V3 & V4
        if Config.AutoV3 then
            if tick() % 1 < 0.1 then -- Spam T every second approx
                VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.T, false, game)
                task.wait(0.05)
                VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(false, Enum.KeyCode.T, false, game)
            end
        end
    end))

    -- AUTO AWAKENING LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.AutoAwakening then
                pcall(function()
                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                    if backpack then
                        local awakening = backpack:FindFirstChild("Awakening")
                        if awakening then
                            local remoteFunc = awakening:FindFirstChild("RemoteFunction")
                            if remoteFunc then remoteFunc:InvokeServer(true) end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end)

    -- DASH LENGTH LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.DashLengthEnabled and character then
                local val = Config.DashLengthValue
                if character:GetAttribute("DashLength") ~= val then
                    character:SetAttribute("DashLength", val)
                    character:SetAttribute("DashLengthAir", val)
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end)

    -- HANDLE EXTENDER LOOP
    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            if Config.HandleExtender then
                local character = player.Character
                if character then
                    local tool = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool")
                    if tool then
                        for _, part in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                if not part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then
                                    part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", part.Size)
                                end
                                part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.HandleSize
                                part.Massless = true
                                part.CanCollide = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    
                    local armParts = {"Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg", "LeftHand", "RightHand", "LeftLowerArm", "LeftUpperArm", "RightLowerArm", "RightUpperArm", "LeftLowerLeg", "LeftUpperLeg", "LeftFoot", "RightLowerLeg", "RightUpperLeg", "RightFoot"}
                    for _, name in pairs(armParts) do
                        local part = character:FindFirstChild(name)
                        if part and part:IsA("BasePart") then
                            if not part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") then part:SetAttribute("OriginalSize", part.Size) end
                            part.Size = part:GetAttribute("OriginalSize") * Config.HandleSize
                            part.Massless = true
                            part.CanCollide = false
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.1)
        end
    end)

    -- Inputs
    table.insert(Connections, UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gp)
        if gp and not (input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R and Config.AirFlashStep) then return end

        -- Air FlashStep: spawn invisible part at mouse world position (clamped by range)
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R and Config.AirFlashStep then
        if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.RightControl then
            if isMinimized then
                restoreGui()
            else
                minimizeGui()
            end
        end

            if character and rootPart then
                local maxDist = Config.AirFlashStepRange or 200
                local mouseHit = mouse.Hit.Position
                local direction = (mouseHit - rootPart.Position).Unit
                local distance = (mouseHit - rootPart.Position).Magnitude
                local targetPos = mouseHit
                if distance > maxDist then targetPos = rootPart.Position + direction * maxDist end
                
                local p = Instance.new("Part")
                p.Anchored = true
                p.CanCollide = false
                p.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
                p.Size = Vector3.new(4, 4, 4)
                p.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPos + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0))
                p.Transparency = 0
                p.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
                p.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0)
                p.Name = "AirFlashStepPart"
                p.Parent = workspace
                task.delay(1, function() if p then p:Destroy() end end)
            end
        end

        if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 and (Config.Reach or Config.HitboxExpander) then
            AttackFunction() -- Force server registration on manual click
        end
        
        -- INTERACT WITH N (Blox Fruits Fix for ClickDetectors)
        if Config.HitboxPreset and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.N then
            if character then
                local root = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if root then
                    local closestObj = nil
                    local minDst = 15
                    for _, v in pairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v:IsA("ClickDetector") and v.Parent and v.Parent:IsA("BasePart") then
                            local dst = (v.Parent.Position - root.Position).Magnitude
                            if dst < minDst then
                                minDst = dst
                                closestObj = v
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if closestObj and fireclickdetector then
                        fireclickdetector(closestObj)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
