        if input.KeyCode == Config.HideGuiKey then
            isGuiVisible = not isGuiVisible
            if isMinimized then
                if MinimizedGui then MinimizedGui.Enabled = isGuiVisible end
            else
                MainFrame.Visible = isGuiVisible
            end
            
            if _G.SnowGui then
                if Config.DisableSnow then
                    _G.SnowGui.Enabled = false
                else
                    _G.SnowGui.Enabled = isGuiVisible
                end
            end
        end
        
        if input.KeyCode == Config.GhostModeKey and Config.GhostModeKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.GhostMode = not Config.GhostMode
            if ToggleButtons["GhostMode"] then
                ToggleButtons["GhostMode"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.GhostMode and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
            if Config.GhostMode then EnableGhostMode() else DisableGhostMode() end
        end
        
        if input.KeyCode == Config.FakeLagKey and Config.FakeLagKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.FakeLag = not Config.FakeLag
            if ToggleButtons["FakeLag"] then
                ToggleButtons["FakeLag"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.FakeLag and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        if input.KeyCode == Config.DesyncKey and Config.DesyncKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.Desync = not Config.Desync
            if Config.Desync then
                enableDesync()
            else
                disableDesync()
            end
            if ToggleButtons["Desync"] then
                ToggleButtons["Desync"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.Desync and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        -- CURSOR LOCK ACTIVATE/CHANGE KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.CursorLockKey and Config.CursorLockKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.CursorLock = true
            
            if ToggleButtons["CursorLock"] then
                ToggleButtons["CursorLock"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
            end
            
            if Config.CursorLockUser == "" then
                local target = getClosestPlayerToMouse(nil, false)
                if target and target.Character then
                    cursorLockTarget = target.Character
                    CursorLabel.Text = "LOCKED: " .. target.Name
                    CursorLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                else
                    CursorLabel.Text = "Status: No Target Found"
                    CursorLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
                end
            else
                CursorLabel.Text = "Searching: " .. Config.CursorLockUser
                CursorLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 0)
            end
        end
        
        -- CURSOR LOCK DISABLE KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.CursorLockDisableKey and Config.CursorLockDisableKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.CursorLock = false
            cursorLockTarget = nil
            
            if ToggleButtons["CursorLock"] then
                ToggleButtons["CursorLock"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
            
            CursorLabel.Text = "Status: Disabled"
            CursorLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
        end
        
        -- AIMLOCK KEY (Manual Toggle)
        if input.KeyCode == Config.AimlockKey and Config.Aimlock and Config.AimlockKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            if aimlockTarget then
                aimlockTarget = nil
            else
                local targetPlr = getClosestPlayerToMouse(nil, false)
                if targetPlr and targetPlr.Character then
                    aimlockTarget = targetPlr.Character
                    aimlockEndTime = math.huge -- Manual lock stays forever until toggled off
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- ZONE LOCK KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.ZoneKey and Config.ZoneKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.ZoneLock = not Config.ZoneLock
            if ToggleButtons["ZoneLock"] then
                ToggleButtons["ZoneLock"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.ZoneLock and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        -- SILENT AIM TOGGLE KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.SilentAimKey and Config.SilentAimKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.SilentAim = not Config.SilentAim
            if ToggleButtons["SilentAim"] then
                ToggleButtons["SilentAim"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.SilentAim and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        -- FARM KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.FarmKey and Config.FarmKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.FarmNearest = not Config.FarmNearest
            if ToggleButtons["FarmNearest"] then
                ToggleButtons["FarmNearest"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.FarmNearest and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
            
            if Config.FarmNearest then
                Config.Reach = true
                Config.ReachSize = 100
                Config.ReachTransparency = 1
                if ToggleButtons["Reach"] then ToggleButtons["Reach"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor end
            else
                Config.Reach = false
                Config.ReachSize = 0
                if ToggleButtons["Reach"] then ToggleButtons["Reach"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) end
            end
        end
        
        -- AUTO RAID KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.AutoRaidKey and Config.AutoRaidKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.AutoRaid = not Config.AutoRaid
            if ToggleButtons["AutoRaid"] then
                ToggleButtons["AutoRaid"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.AutoRaid and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
            if Config.AutoRaid then
                 Config.AntiLava = true
                 if ToggleButtons["AntiLava"] then ToggleButtons["AntiLava"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor end
            end
        end
        
        -- ONE SHOT KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.OneShotKey and Config.OneShotKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            if isOneShotActive then
                isOneShotActive = false
                if oneShotThread then task.cancel(oneShotThread); oneShotThread = nil end
            else
                stopTeleport()
                isOneShotActive = true
                oneShotThread = task.spawn(function()
                    while isOneShotActive do
                        if character and rootPart then rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(937.95, 251.42, 32886.68) end
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
        
        -- PANIC MODE KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.PanicModeKey and Config.PanicModeKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.PanicMode = not Config.PanicMode
            -- Disable Auto Panic if manual toggle is used to prevent conflict
            if Config.PanicModeHealthEnable then
                Config.PanicModeHealthEnable = false
                if ToggleButtons["PanicModeHealthEnable"] then
                    ToggleButtons["PanicModeHealthEnable"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                end
                SendNotification("Auto Panic disabled for manual control", 2)
            end
            if ToggleButtons["PanicMode"] then
                ToggleButtons["PanicMode"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.PanicMode and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        -- ORBIT PLAYER KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.OrbitPlayerKey and Config.OrbitPlayerKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.OrbitPlayer = not Config.OrbitPlayer
            if ToggleButtons["OrbitPlayer"] then
                ToggleButtons["OrbitPlayer"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.OrbitPlayer and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        -- ORBIT PLAYER KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.OrbitPlayerKey and Config.OrbitPlayerKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.OrbitPlayer = not Config.OrbitPlayer
            if ToggleButtons["OrbitPlayer"] then
                ToggleButtons["OrbitPlayer"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.OrbitPlayer and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
        end
        
        if Config.InfJump and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
            humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
        end
        
        -- SPEED KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.SpeedKey and Config.SpeedKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.SpeedHack = not Config.SpeedHack
        end
        
        -- FLY KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.StandardFlyKey and Config.StandardFlyKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.StandardFly = not Config.StandardFly
        end
        
        -- LOCK KEY (AUTO AURA SYNC)
        if input.KeyCode == Config.LockKey and Config.LockKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            Config.EasyLock = not Config.EasyLock
            if ToggleButtons["EasyLock"] then
                ToggleButtons["EasyLock"].BackgroundColor3 = Config.EasyLock and CurrentThemeColor or Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
            end
            
            if Config.EasyLock then
                -- LOCK
                local target = getClosestPlayerToMouse(nil, false) -- No FOV limit for hard lock
                if target then
                    Config.TargetName = target.Name
                    TargetLabel.Text = "LOCKED: " .. target.Name
                    TargetLabel.TextColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    
                    -- AUTO ENABLE AURA
                    Config.KillAura = true
                    if ToggleButtons["KillAura"] then
                        ToggleButtons["KillAura"].BackgroundColor3 = CurrentThemeColor
                    end
                else
                    Config.EasyLock = false
                    if ToggleButtons["EasyLock"] then ToggleButtons["EasyLock"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50) end
                end
            else
                -- UNLOCK
                Config.TargetName = "None"
                TargetLabel.Text = "Status: Unlocked"
                TargetLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
                local bv = rootPart:FindFirstChild("FlyVelocity")
                if bv then bv:Destroy() end
                
                -- AUTO DISABLE AURA
                Config.KillAura = false
                if ToggleButtons["KillAura"] then
                    ToggleButtons["KillAura"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- TP PLAYER KEY
        if input.KeyCode == Config.TPPlayerKey and Config.TPPlayerKey ~= Enum.KeyCode.Unknown then
            local targetChar = nil
            
            -- 1. Try Mouse Target (Direct Aim)
            local mouseTarget = mouse.Target
            if mouseTarget and mouseTarget.Parent then
                 local plr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(mouseTarget.Parent)
                 if plr and plr ~= player then targetChar = mouseTarget.Parent end
            end
            
            -- 2. Fallback to closest to mouse
            if not targetChar then
                local p = getClosestPlayerToMouse(math.huge, false)
                if p then targetChar = p.Character end
            end
            
            if targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and rootPart then
                local dist = (targetChar.HumanoidRootPart.Position - rootPart.Position).Magnitude
                if dist <= Config.TPPlayerRange then
                    -- Teleport behind player
                    rootPart.CFrame = targetChar.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 3)
                end
            end
        end
    end))

    table.insert(Connections, player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
        character = newChar
        rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10)
        humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10)
        character.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child) restoreToolColor(child) end)
        
        -- Reset fly on respawn
        Config.StandardFly = false
        if ToggleButtons["StandardFly"] then
            ToggleButtons["StandardFly"].BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 50)
        end
        
        -- Force IMMEDIATE cleanup of all fly-related objects and states
        local newRoot = newChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if newRoot then
            -- Destroy all fly-related velocity/gyro objects
            for _, obj in pairs(newRoot:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("BodyVelocity") or obj:IsA("BodyGyro") or obj:IsA("BodyPosition") then
                    if obj.Name == "FlyVelocity" or obj.Name == "FlyGyro" or obj.Name == "FarmVelocity" then
                        obj:Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        local hum = newChar:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
        if hum then
            hum.PlatformStand = false
            hum.Sit = false
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Landed)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead)
            hum:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
            -- Reset health to max
            hum.Health = hum.MaxHealth
        end
        
        -- Re-apply Infinite FlashStep if enabled
        task.wait(0.5)
        if Config.InfiniteFlashStep then
            newChar:SetAttribute("FlashstepCooldown", 10)
        end
        
        -- Re-apply Infinite Zoom if enabled
        if Config.InfiniteZoom then
            player.CameraMaxZoomDistance = 100000
            player.CameraMinZoomDistance = 0.5
        end
        
        -- Re-apply Ice Water if enabled
        if Config.IceWater then
            newChar:SetAttribute("WaterWalking", true)
        end
        
        -- Re-apply Unbreakable All if enabled
        if Config.UnbreakableAll then
            newChar:SetAttribute("UnbreakableAll", true)
        end
        
        if Config.InstantRespawn then
            BindInstantRespawn()
        end
        
        combatTarget = nil
        cursorLockTarget = nil
        hakiAttempted = false
        if reachConnection then
            reachConnection:Disconnect()
            reachConnection = nil
        end
    end))

    WatchForNewTools()

    table.insert(Connections, player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
        originalWeaponSizes = {}
        task.wait(1)
        WatchForNewTools()
        if Config.WeaponExtender then
            SetWeaponSize(Config.WeaponLength)
        end
    end))

    task.spawn(function()
        while Config.IsRunning do
            task.wait(0.1)
            if Config.WeaponExtender then
                SetWeaponSize(Config.WeaponLength)
            end
        end
    end)

    table.insert(Connections, RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
        if Config.WeaponExtender then
            local character = player.Character
            if character then
                for _, tool in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
                    if tool:IsA("Tool") then
                        local handle = tool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
                        if handle and handle:IsA("BasePart") then
                            local compensationMultiplier = Config.WeaponLength
                            if Config.SizeMultiplierEnabled then
                                compensationMultiplier = Config.WeaponLength * Config.SizeMultiplier
                            end
                            
                            if originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name] and originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name].HandleSize then
                                handle.Size = originalWeaponSizes[tool.Name].HandleSize * compensationMultiplier
                                handle.CanCollide = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end))

    if character then
        character.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(child) restoreToolColor(child) end)
    end
end


-- === SNOW EFFECT ===
_G.SnowGui = nil
local SnowConnections = {}
local SnowEnabled = true
local isSnowActive = true -- Track if snow should be shown (not minimized)

-- Customizable colors (modify these to change colors)
_G.SnowFlakeColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) -- Snowflake color (default: white)
_G.SnowBackgroundColor = Color3.fromRGB(10, 10, 15) -- Background color (default: dark blue/black)

function updateSnowColors()
    -- Create snow if it doesn't exist
    if not _G.SnowGui then createSnow() end
    if not _G.SnowGui then return end
    
    -- Update background frame
    for _, child in ipairs(_G.SnowGui:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Frame") and child.Name == "BackgroundFrame" then
            child.BackgroundColor3 = _G.SnowBackgroundColor
        end
    end
    
    -- Update global snowflakes array
    if _G.Snowflakes then
        for _, flake in ipairs(_G.Snowflakes) do
            if flake.frame then
                flake.frame.BackgroundColor3 = _G.SnowFlakeColor
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Also update any existing GUI elements
    local SnowContainer = _G.SnowGui:FindFirstChild("SnowContainer")
    if SnowContainer then
        for _, child in ipairs(SnowContainer:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("Frame") then
                child.BackgroundColor3 = _G.SnowFlakeColor
            end
        end
    end
end

function createSnow()
   print("snowflakes")
   end

createSnow()
updateSnowColors()

-- Function to change snow colors (call this to customize)
-- Example: _G.SetSnowColors(Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100), Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 50))
_G.SetSnowColors = function(flakeColor, backgroundColor)
    _G.SnowFlakeColor = flakeColor or Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    _G.SnowBackgroundColor = backgroundColor or Color3.fromRGB(10, 10, 15)
    updateSnowColors()
end

-- Hook into minimize/restore to hide/show snow (must be after ShowKeySystem)
if minimizeGui and restoreGui then
    local origMinimizeGui = minimizeGui
    minimizeGui = function()
        if _G.SnowGui then _G.SnowGui.Enabled = false end
        origMinimizeGui()
    end

    local origRestoreGui = restoreGui
    restoreGui = function()
        origRestoreGui()
        if _G.SnowGui then _G.SnowGui.Enabled = true end
    end
end

-- Update destroy function to clean up snow
local origDestroyCheat = DestroyCheat
DestroyCheat = function()
    if _G.SnowGui then _G.SnowGui:Destroy() end
    _G.SnowGui = nil
    _G.Snowflakes = nil
    for _, c in pairs(SnowConnections) do if c then c:Disconnect() end end
    SnowConnections = {}
    if origDestroyCheat then
        origDestroyCheat()
    end
end

StartCheat(999999999, "Bypassed", true)
